Oṃ Śrīmad Ānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracitaḥ
Śrī Mahābhāratatātparyanirṇayaḥ
atha prathamo'dhyāyaḥ
sarvaśāstratātparyanirṇayaḥ 
Oṃ  nārāyaṇāya paripūrṇaguṇārṇavāya viśvodayasthitilayonniyatipradāya 
j ñānapradāya vibudhāsurasaukhyaduḥkhasatkāraṇāya vitatāya namo namaste   
āsīdudāraguṇavāridhiraprameyo nārāyaṇaḥ paratamaḥ paramāt sa ekaḥ 
saṃ śāntasaṃ vidakhilaṃ jaṭhare nidhāya lakṣmībhujāntaragataḥ svarato'pi cāgre   
tasyodarasthajagataḥ sadamandasāndrasvānandatuṣṭavapuṣo'pi ramāramasya 
bhūtyai nijāṇsritajanasya hi sṛjyasṛṣṭāvīkṣā babhūva paranāmanimeṣakānte   
dṛṣṭvā sa cetanagaṇān jaṭhare śayānānānandamātravapuṣaḥ sṛtivipramuktān 
dhyānaṃ gatān sṛtigatāṃ śca suṣuptisaṃ sthān brahmādikān kaliparān manujāṃ stathaikṣat   
srakṣye hi cetanagaṇān sukhaduḥkhamadhyasamprāptaye tanubhṛt āṃ vihṛtiṃ mamecchan 
so'yaṃ vihāra iha me tanubhṛt svabhāvasambhūtaye bhavati bhūtikṛdeva bhūtyāḥ   
itthaṃ vicintya paramaḥ sa tu vāsudevanāmā babhūva nijamuktipadapradātā 
tasyājñayaiva niyatā'tha ramā'pi rūpaṃ babhre dvitīyamapi yat pravadanti māyām   
saṅkarṣaṇaṇsca sa babhūva punaḥ sunityaḥ saṃ hārakāraṇavapustadanujñayaiva 
devī jayetyanu babhūva sa sṛṣṭihetoḥ pradyumnatāmupagataḥ kṛtitāṃ ca devī   
sthityai punaḥ sa bhagavānaniruddhanāmā devī caśāntirabhavaccharadāṃ sahasram 
sthitvā svamūrtibhiramūbhiracintyaśaktiḥ pradyumnarūpaka imāṃ ścaramātmane'dāt   
nirdehakān sa bhagavānaniruddhanāmā jīvān svakarmasahitān udare niveśya 
cakre'tha dehasahitān kramaśaḥ svayambhuprāṇātmaśeṣagaruḍeṇsamukhān samagrān   
pañcātmakaḥ sa bhagavān dviṣaḍātmako'bhūt pañcadvayī śatasahasraparo'mitaśca 
iekaḥ samo'pyakhiladoṣasamujjhito'pi sarvatra pūrṇaguṇako'pi bahūpamo'bhūt   
nirdoṣapūrṇaguṇavigraha ātmatantro niścetanātmakaśarīraguṇaiśca hīnaḥ 
ānandamātrakarapādamukhodarādiḥ sarvatra ca svagatabhedavivarjitātmā   
kālācca deśaguṇato'sya na cā'diranto vṛddhikṣayau na tu parasya sadātanasya 
naitādṛśaḥ kva ca babhūva na caiva bhāvyo nāstyuttaraḥ kimu parāt paramasya viṣṇoḥ   
sarvajña īśvaratamaḥ sa ca sarvaśaktiḥ pūrṇāvyayātmabalacitsukhavīryasāraḥ 
yasyā'jñayā rahitamindirayā sametaṃ brahmeśapūrvakamidaṃ na tu kasya ceśam   
ābhāsako'sya pavanaḥ pavanasya rudraḥ śeṣātmako garuḍa eva ca śakrakāmau 
vīndreśayostadapare tvanayośca teṣāṃ ṛṣyādayaḥ kramaśa ūnaguṇāḥ śatāṃ śāḥ   
ābhāsakā tvatha ramā'sya marutsvarūpācchreṣṭhā'pyajāt tadanu gīḥ śivato variṣṭhā 
tasyā umā vipatinī ca girastayo'stu śacyādikāḥ kramaśa eva yathā pumāṃ saḥ   
t ābhyaśca te śataguṇairdaśato variṣṭhāḥ pañcottarairapi yathākramataḥ śrutisthāḥ 
śabdo bahutvavacanaḥ śatamityataśca śrutyantareṣu bahudhoktiviruddhatā na  
teṣāṃ svarūpamidameva yato'tha muktā apyevameva satatoccavinīcarūpāḥ 
śabdaḥ śataṃ daśasahasramiti sma yasmāt tasmānna hīnavacano'tha tato'gryarūpāḥ   
evaṃ narottamaparāstu vimuktiyogyā anye ca saṃ sṛtiparā asurāstamogāḥ 
evaṃ sadaiva niyamaḥ kvacidanyathā nayāvanna pūrtiruta saṃ sṛtigāḥ samastāḥ   
pūrtiśca naiva niyamād bhavitā hi yasmāt tasmāt samāptimapi yānti na jīvasa' nghāḥ 
ānantyameva gaṇaṇso'sti yato hi teṣāṃ itthaṃ tataḥ sakalakālagatā pravṛttiḥ   
etaiḥ surādibhiratipratibhādiyuktairyuktaiḥ sahaiva satataṃ pravicintayadbhiḥ 
pūrteracintyamahimaḥ paramaḥ parātmā nārāyaṇo'sya guṇavistṛtiranyagā kva   
sāmyaṃ na cāsya paramasya ca kena cā'pyaṃ muktena ca kvacidatastvabhidā kuto'sya 
prāpyeta cetanagaṇaiḥ satatāsvatantrairnityasvatantravapuṣaḥ paramāt parasya   
iiartho'yameva nikhilairapi vedavākyai rāmāyaṇaiḥ sahitabhāratapañcarātraiḥ 
anyaiśca śāstravacanaiḥ sahatattvasūtrairnirṇīyate sahṛdayaṃ hariṇā sadaiva   
'nārāyaṇasya na samaḥ ' 'puruṣottamo'haṃ
jīvākṣare hyatigato'smi' tato 'nyadārtam 
mukto'pasṛpya 'iha nāsti kutaśca kaścit'
nāneva 'dharmapṛthagātmadṛgetyadho hi'   
ābhāsa eva 'pṛthagīśata eṣa jīvo'
'muktasya nāsti jagato viṣaye tu śaktiḥ ' 
'mātrāparo'si na tu te'śnuvate mahitvaṃ '
'ṣāḍguṇyavigraha' 'supūrṇaguṇaikadehaḥ '   
'māhātmyadeha' 'sṛtimuktigate' 'śivaśca brahmā
ca tadguṇagatau na kathañcaneśau' 
'na śrīḥ kutastadapare' ''sya sukhasya mātrāmaṇ
snanti muktasugaṇāṇsca śatāvareṇa'   
ābhāsakābhāsaparāvabhāsarūpāṇyajasrāṇi ca cetanānām 
viṣṇoḥ sadaivāti vaśāt kadāpi gacchanti keśādigaṇā na muktau    
'yasmin pare'nye'pyajajīvakośā'
'nāhaṃ parāyurna marīcimukhyāḥ ' 
'jānanti yadguṇagaṇān na ramādayo'pi
nityasvatantra uta ko'sti tadanya īśaḥ '   
'naivaika eva puruṣaḥ puruṣottamo'sāvekah
 kutaḥ sa puruṣo' 'yata eva jātyā 
arthāt śruteśca guṇato nijarūpataśca
nityānya eva kathamasmi sa ityapi syāt'   
 Bṛ U 
 Bra Sū

 Bra Sū 
 Ḹabhāsaka ityādi śrutivacanameva 
na svavacanam  Bhā Pra
iii'sarvottamo hariridaṃ tu tadājñayaiva
cettuṃ kṣamaṃ sa tu hariḥ paramasvatantraḥ 
pūrṇāvyayāgaṇitanityaguṇārṇavo'sau'
ityeva vedavacanāni paroktayaśca   
ṛgādayaśca catvāraḥ pañcarātraṃ ca bhāratam 
mūlarāmāyaṇaṃ brahmasūtraṃ mānaṃ svataḥ smṛtam   
aviruddhaṃ ca yattvasya pramāṇaṃ tacca nānyathā 
etadviruddhaṃ yattu syānna tanmānaṃ kathañcana   
vaiṣṇavāni purāṇāni pañcarātrātmakatvataḥ 
pramāṇānyeva manvādyāḥ smṛtayo'pyanukūlataḥ   
eteṣu viṣṇorādhikyamucyate'nyasya na kvacit 
atastadeva mantavyaṃ nānyathā tu kathañcana   
mohārthānyanyaśāstrāṇi kṛt ānyevā'jñayā hareḥ 
atasteṣūktamagrāhyamasurāṇāṃ tamogateḥ   
yasmāt kṛt āni tānīha viṣṇunoktaiḥ śivādibhiḥ 
eṣāṃ yanna virodhi syāt tatroktaṃ tanna vāryate   
viṣṇvādhikyavirodhīni yāni vedavacāṃ syapi 
t āni yojyānyānukūlyād viṣṇvādhikyasya sarvaśaḥ   
avatāreṣu yat kiñcid darśayennaravaddhariḥ 
taccāsurāṇāṃ mohāya doṣā viṣṇornahi kvacit   
ajñatvaṃ pāravaśyaṃ vā vedhabhedādikaṃ tathā 
tathā prākṛtadehatvaṃ dehatyāgādikaṃ tathā   
anīśatvaṃ ca duḥkhitvaṃ sāmyamanyaiśca hīnatām 
pradarśayati mohāya daityādīnāṃ hariḥ svayam   
ivna tasya kaścid doṣo'sti pūrṇākhilaguṇo hyasau 
sarvadehastharūpeṣu prādurbhāveṣu ceśvaraḥ   
brahmādyabhedaḥ sāmyaṃ vā kutastasya mahātmanaḥ 
yadevaṃ vācakaṃ śāstraṃ taddhi śāstraṃ paraṃ matam   
nirṇayāyaiva yat proktaṃ brahmasūtraṃ tu viṣṇunā 
vyāsarūpeṇa tad grāhyaṃ tatroktāḥ sarvanirṇayāḥ   
yathārthavacanānāṃ ca mohārthānāṃ ca saṃ śayam 
apanetuṃ hi bhagavān brahmasūtramacīklṛpat   
tasmāt sūtrārthamāgṛhya kartavyaḥ sarvanirṇayaḥ 
sarvadoṣavihīnatvaṃ guṇaiḥ sarvairudīrṇatā   
abhedaḥ sarvarūpeṣu jīvabhedaḥ sadaiva ca 
viṣṇoruktāni sūtreṣu sarvavedeḍyatā tathā   
t āratamyaṃ ca muktānāṃ vimuktirvidyayā tathā 
tasmādetadviruddhaṃ yanmohāya tadudāhṛtam   
tasmād ye ye guṇā viṣṇorgrāhyāste sarva eva tu 
ityādyuktaṃ bhagavatā bhaviṣyatparvaṇi sphuṭam   
eṣa mohaṃ sṛj āmyāṇsu yo janān mohayiṣyati 
tvaṃ ca rudra mahābāho mohaśāstrāṇi kāraya   
atatthyāni vitatthyāni darśayasva mahābhuja 
prakāṇsaṃ kuru cā'tmānamaprakāṇsaṃ ca māṃ kuru   
iti vārāhavacanaṃ brahmāṇḍoktaṃ tathā'param 
amohāya guṇā viṣṇorākāraściccharīratā   
nirdoṣatvaṃ t āratamyaṃ muktānāmapi cocyate 
etadviruddhaṃ yat sarvaṃ tanmohāya iti nirṇayaḥ    
vskānde'pyuktaṃ śivenaiva ṣaṇmukhāyaiva sādaram 
śivaśāstre'pi tad grāhyaṃ bhagavacchāstrayogi yat   
paramo viṣṇurevaikastajjñānaṃ mokṣasādhanam 
śāstrāṇāṃ nirṇayastveṣa tadanyanmohanāya hi   
j ñānaṃ vinā tuyā muktiḥ sāmyaṃ ca mama viṣṇunā 
tīrthā'dimātrato jñānaṃ mamā'dhikyaṃ ca viṣṇutaḥ   
abhedaścāsmadādīnāṃ muktānāṃ hariṇā tathā 
ityādi sarvaṃ mohāya kathyate putra nānyathā   
uktaṃ pādmapurāṇe caśaiva eva śivena tu 
yaduktaṃ hariṇā pūrvaṃ umāyai prāha taddharaḥ   
tvāmārādhya tathā ṇsambho grahīṣyāmi varaṃ sadā 
dvāparā'dau yuge bhūtvā kalayā mānuṣā'diṣu   
svā'gamaiḥ kalpitaistvaṃ ca janān madvimukhān kuru 
māṃ ca gopāya yena syāt sṛṣṭireṣottarādharā   
na ca vaiṣṇavaśāstreṣu vedeṣvapi hareḥ paraḥ 
kvacidukto'nyaśāstreṣu paramo viṣṇurīritaḥ  
nirdoṣatvācca vedānāṃ vedoktaṃ grāhyameva hi 
vedeṣu ca paro viṣṇuḥ sarvasmāducyate sadā   
asya devasya mīl  huṣo vayā viṣṇoreṣasya prabhṛthe havirbhiḥ 
vide hi rudro rudriyaṃ mahitvaṃ yāsiṣṭaṃ vartiraśvanāvirāvat

 Ṛgveda 
vistuhi śrutaṃ gartasadaṃ yuvānaṃ mṛgaṃ na bhīmam upahatnumugram 
yaṃ kāmaye taṃ tamugraṃ kṛṇomi taṃ brahmāṇaṃ tamṛṣiṃ taṃ sumedhām   
eko nārāyaṇa āsīnna brahmā na caśaṅkaraḥ  
vāsudevo vā idamagra āsīnna brahmā na caśaṅkaraḥ    
yadā paśyaḥ paśyate rugmavarṇaṃ kartāramīśaṃ puruṣaṃ brahmayonim 
tadā vidvān puṇyapāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramaṃ sāmyamupaiti   
yo veda nihitaṃ guhāyāṃ parame vyoman 
so'śnute sarvān kāmān saha brahmaṇā vipaścitā   
pra ghā nvasya mahato mahāni satyā satyasya karaṇāni vocam 
satyamenaṃ anu viśve madanti rātiṃ devasya gṛṇato maghonaḥ     
yacciketa satyamit tan na moghaṃ vasu spārhamuta jeto'ta dātā 
satyaḥ so asya mahimā gṛṇe ṇsavo yajñeṣu viprarājye   
satyā viṣṇorguṇāḥ sarve satyā jīveśayorbhidā 
satyo mitho jīvabhedaḥ satyaṃ ca jagadīdṛśam   
asatyaḥ svagato bhedo viṣṇornānyadasatyakam 
jagatpravāhaḥ satyo'yaṃ pañcabhedasamanvitaḥ   
jīveśayorbhidā caiva jīvabhedaḥ parasparam 
jaḍeṇsayorjaḍānāṃ ca jaḍajīvabhidā tathā   
pañcabhedā ime nityāḥ sarvāvasthāsu sarvaśaḥ

 Ṛgveda 
viimuktānāṃ ca na hīyante tāratamyaṃ ca sarvadā   
kṣitipā manuṣyagandharvā daivāṇsca pitaraścirāḥ 
ājānajāḥ karmajāṇsca devā indraḥ purandaraḥ   
rudraḥ sarasvatī vāyurmuktāḥ śataguṇottarāḥ 
eko brahmā ca vāyuśca vīndro rudrasamastathā 
eko rudrastathā ṇseṣo nakaścidvāyunā samaḥ   
mukteṣu ṇsrīstathā vāyoḥ sahasraguṇit ā guṇaiḥ 
tato'nantaguṇo viṣṇurna kaścit tatsamaḥ sadā   
ityādi vedavākyaṃ viṣṇorutkarṣameva vaktyuccaiḥ 
t ātparyaṃ mahadatretyuktaṃ yo mām iti svayaṃ tena   
bhūmno jyāyastvam iti hyuktaṃ sūtreṣu nirṇayāt tena  
tatprītyaiva ca mokṣaḥ prāpyastenaiva nānyena   
nāyamātmā pravacanena labhyo na medhayā na bahunā ṇsrutena 
yamevaiṣa vṛṇute tena labhyastasyaiṣa ātmā vivṛṇute tanuṃ svām   
viṣṇurhi dātā mokṣasya vāyuśca tadanujñayā 
mokṣo jñānaṃ ca kramaśo muktigo bhoga eva ca   
uttareṣāṃ prasādena nīcānāṃ nānyathā bhavet 
sarveṣāṃ ca harirnityaṃ niyantā tadvaśāḥ pare   
t āratamyaṃ tato jñeyaṃ sarvoccatvaṃ harestathā 
etadvinā na kasyāpi vimuktiḥ syāt kathañcana

 Ka U  Mu U 
viiipañcabhedāṃ śca vijñāya viṣṇoḥ svābhedameva ca 
nirdoṣatvaṃ guṇādrekaṃ j ñātvā muktirnacānyathā   
avatārān harerjñātvā nāvatārā hareśca ye 
tadāveśāṃ stathā samyag jñātvā muktirnacānyathā   
sṛṣṭirakṣā'hṛtijñānaniyatyajñānabandhanān 
mokṣaṃ ca viṣṇutastveva jñātvā muktirnacānyathā   
vedāṃ śca pañcarātrāṇi setihāsapurāṇakān 
j ñātvā viṣṇuparāneva mucyate nānyathā kvacit   
māhātmyajñānapūrvastu sudṛḍhaḥ sarvato'dhikaḥ 
sneho bhaktiriti proktaḥ tayā muktirnacānyathā   
trividhā jīvasa' nghāstu devamānuṣadānavāḥ 
tatra devā muktiyogyā mānuṣeṣūttamāstathā   
madhyamā mānuṣā yetu sṛtiyogyāḥ sadaiva hi 
adhamā nirayāyaiva dānavāstu tamolayāḥ   
muktirnityā tamaścaiva nā'vṛttiḥ punaretayoḥ 
devānāṃ nirayo nāsti tamaścāpi kathañcana   
nāsurāṇāṃ tathā muktiḥ kadācit kenacit kvacit 
mānuṣāṇāṃ madhyamānāṃ naivaitaddvayamāpyate   
asurāṇāṃ tamaḥ prāptistadā niyamato bhavet 
yadā tujñānisadbhāve naiva gṛhṇanti tatparam   
tadā muktiśca devānāṃ yadā pratyakṣago hariḥ 
svayogyayopāsanayā tanvā tadyogyayā tathā   
sarvairguṇairbrahmaṇā tu samupāsyo hariḥ sadā 
ixānando jñaḥ sadātmeti hyupāsyo mānuṣairhariḥ   
yathākramaṃ guṇodrekāt tadanyairā viriñcataḥ 
brahmatvayogyā ṛjavo nāma devāḥ pṛthaggaṇāḥ   
tairevāpyaṃ padaṃ tattu naivānyaiḥ sādhanairapi 
evaṃ sarvapadānāṃ tu yogyāḥ santi pṛthag gaṇāḥ   
tasmādanādyanantaṃ hi tāratamyaṃ cidātmanām 
tacca naivānyathā kartuṃ śakyaṃ kenāpi kutracit   
ayogyamicchan puruṣaḥ patatyeva na saṃ śayaḥ 
tasmād yogyānusāreṇa sevyo viṣṇuḥ sadaiva hi   
acchidrasevanāccaiva niṣkāmatvācca yogyataḥ 
draṣṭuṃ śakyo hariḥ sarvairnānyathā tu kathañcana   
niyamo'yaṃ hareryasmānnollaṅghyaḥ sarvacetanaiḥ 
satyasaṅkalpato viṣṇurnānyathā ca kariṣyati   
dānatīrthatapoyajñapūrvāḥ sarve'pi sarvadā 
aṅgāni harisevāyāṃ bhaktistvekā vimuktaye 
bhaviṣyatparvavacanamityetadakhilaṃ param   
ṇsṛṇve vīra ugramugraṃ damāyannanyamanyaṃ atinenīyamānaḥ 
edhamānadvil  ubhayasya rājā coṣkūyate viśa indro manuṣyān   
parā pūrveṣāṃ sakhyā vṛṇakti vitarturāṇo aparebhireti 
anānubhūtīravadhūnvānaḥ pūrvīrindraḥ śaradastartarīti   
tamevaṃ vidvānamṛta iha bhavati nānyaḥ panthā ayanāya vidyate

 Tai Ā 
xtameva viditvā'ti mṛtyumeti nānyaḥ panthā vidyate'yanāya   
yasya deve parā bhaktiryathādeve tathā gurau 
tasyaite kathitā hyarthāḥ prakāṇsante mahātmanaḥ     
bhaktyarthānyakhilānyeva bhaktirmokṣāya kevalā 
muktānāmapi bhaktirhi nityānandasvarūpiṇī   
j ñānapūrvaḥ paraḥ sneho nityo bhaktiritīryate 
ityādi vedavacanaṃ sādhanapravidhāyakam   
niśśeṣadharmakartā'pyabhaktaste narake hare 
sadā tiṣṭhati bhaktaśced brahmahā'pi vimucyate   
dharmo bhavatyadharmo'pi kṛto bhaktaistavā'cyuta 
pāpaṃ bhavati dharmo'pi yo na bhaktaiḥ kṛto hare   
bhaktyā tvananyayā ṇsakya ahamevaṃ vidho'rjuna 
j ñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca tattvena praveṣṭuṃ ca parantapa   
anādidveṣiṇo daityā viṣṇau dveṣo vivardhitaḥ 
tamasyandhe pātayati daityānante viniścayāt   
pūrṇaduḥkhātmako dveṣaḥ so'nanto hyavatiṣṭhate 
patitānāṃ tamasyandhe niḥ śeṣasukhavarjite   
jīvābhedo nirguṇatvaṃ apūrṇaguṇatā tathā 
sāmyādhikye tadanyeṣāṃ bhedastadgata eva ca   
prādurbhāvaviparyāsastadbhaktadveṣa eva ca 
tatpramāṇasya nindā ca dveṣā ete'khilā matāḥ

anādibhaktirdevānāṃ kramād vṛddhiṃ gataiva sā   
aparokṣadṛśerheturmuktihetuśca sā punaḥ 
saivā'nandasvarūpeṇa nityā mukteṣu tiṣṭhati   
yathā ṇsauklyādikaṃ rūpaṃ gorbhavatyeva sarvadā 
sukhajñānādikaṃ rūpaṃ evaṃ bhakterna cānyathā   
bhaktyaiva tuṣṭimabhyeti viṣṇurnānyena kenacit 
sa eva muktidātā ca bhaktistatraikakāraṇam   
brahmādīnāṃ ca muktānāṃ t āratamye tu kāraṇam 
t āratamyasthitā'nādinityā bhaktirna cetarat   
mānuṣeṣvadhamāḥ kiñcid dveṣayuktāḥ sadā harau 
duḥkhaniṣṭhāstataste'pi nityameva na saṃ śayaḥ   
madhyamā miśrabhūtatvānnityaṃ miśraphalāḥ smṛt āḥ 
kiñcidbhaktiyutā nityaṃ uttamāstena mokṣiṇaḥ   
brahmaṇaḥ paramā bhaktiḥ sarvebhyaḥ paramastataḥ  
ityādīni ca vākyāni purāṇeṣu pṛthak pṛthak   
ṣaṇṇavatyaṅgulo yastu nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalaḥ 
saptapādaścaturhasto dvātriṃ śallakṣaṇairyutaḥ 
asaṃ śayaḥ saṃ śayacchid gururukto manīṣibhiḥ   
tasmād brahmā gururmukhyaḥ sarveṣāmeva sarvadā 
anye'pi svātmano mukhyāḥ kramād gurava īritāḥ   
kramāllakṣaṇahīnāṇsca lakṣaṇālakṣaṇaiḥ samāḥ 
mānuṣā madhyamāḥ samyag durlakṣaṇayutaḥ kaliḥ   
xiisamyaglakṣaṇasampanno yad dadyāt suprasannadhīḥ 
śiṣyāya satyaṃ bhavati tatsarvaṃ nātra saṃ śayaḥ   
agamyatvāddharistasminnāviṣṭo muktido bhavet 
nātiprasannahṛdayo yad dadyād gururapyasau 
na tat satyaṃ bhavet tasmād arcanīyo guruḥ sadā   
svāvarāṇāṃ gurutvaṃ tu bhavet kāraṇataḥ kvacit 
maryādārthaṃ te'pi pūjyā na tu yadvat paro guruḥ  
ityetat pañcarātroktaṃ purāṇeṣvanumoditam   
yadā muktipradānasya svayogyaṃ paśyati dhruvam 
rūpaṃ harestadā tasya sarvapāpāni bhasmasāt   
yānti pūrvāṇyuttarāṇi naśleṣaṃ yānti kānicit 
mokṣaṇsca niyatastasmāt svayogyaharidarśane   
bhaviṣyatparvavacanamityetat sūtragaṃ tathā  
śrutiśca tatparā tadvat tadyathā ityavadat sphuṭam   
muktāstu mānuṣā devān devā indraṃ sa śaṅkaram 
sa brahmāṇaṃ krameṇaiva tena yāntyakhilā harim   
uttarottaravaśyāṇsca muktā rudrapurassarāḥ 
nirdoṣā nityasukhinaḥ punarāvṛttivarjitāḥ 
svecchayaiva ramante'tra nāniṣṭaṃ teṣu kiñcana   
asurāḥ kaliparyantā evaṃ duḥkhottarottarāḥ 
kalirduḥkhādhikasteṣu te'pyevaṃ brahmavad gaṇāḥ

iti ṛgyajuḥ sāmātharvapañcarātretihāsataḥ

ānandatīrthamuninā pūrṇaprajñābhidhāyujā

vākyoddhāraḥ 
Oṃ  jayati hariracintyaḥ sarvadevaikavandyaḥ paramagururabhīṣṭāvāptidaḥ sajjanānām 
nikhilaguṇagaṇārṇo nityanirmuktadoṣaḥ sarasijanayano'sau śrīpatirmānado naḥ   
uktaḥ pūrve'dhyāye śāstrāṇāṃ nirṇayaḥ paro divyaḥ 
śrīmadbhāratavākyānyetairevādhyavasyante   
kvacid granthān prakṣipanti kvacidantaritānapi 
kuryuḥ kvacicca vyatyāsaṃ pramādāt kvacidanyathā   
anutsannā api granthā vyākulā iti sarvaśaḥ 
utsannāḥ prāyaśaḥ sarve koṭyaṃ śo'pi na vartate   
grantho'pyevaṃ vilul  itaḥ kimvartho devadurgamaḥ 
kalāvevaṃ vyākulite nirṇayāya pracoditaḥ   
hariṇā nirṇayān vacmi vijānaṃ statprasādataḥ 
śāstrāntarāṇi sañjānan vedāṃ ścāsya prasādataḥ   
deśe deśe tathā granthān dṛṣṭvā caiva pṛthagvidhān 
yathā sa bhagavān vyāsaḥ sākṣānnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ   
jagāda bhāratādyeṣu tathā vakṣye tadīkṣayā 
saṅkṣepāt sarvaśāstrārthaṃ bhāratārthānusārataḥ 
nirṇayaḥ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ bhārataṃ parikīrtitam   
bhārataṃ sarvavedāṇsca tulāmāropitāḥ purā 
devairbrahmādibhiḥ sarvairṛṣibhiśca samanvitaiḥ 
vyāsasyaivā'jñayā tatra tvatyaricyata bhāratam   
mahatvād bhāravatvācca mahābhāratamucyate 
xvniruktamasya yo veda sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate   
nirṇayaḥ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ sadṛṣṭānto hi bhārate 
kṛto viṣṇuvaśatvaṃ hi brahmādīnāṃ prakāṇsitam   
yataḥ kṛṣṇavaśe sarve bhīmādyāḥ samyagīritāḥ 
sarveṣāṃ j ñānado viṣṇuryaśodāteti coditaḥ   
yasmādvyāsātmanā teṣāṃ bhārate yaśa ūcivān 
j ñānadaśca śukādīnāṃ brahmarudrādirūpiṇām   
brahmādhikaśca devebhyaḥ śeṣādrudrādapīritaḥ 
priyaśca viṣṇoḥ sarvebhya iti bhīmanidarśanāt   
bhūbhārahāriṇo viṣṇoḥ pradhānāṅgaṃ hi mārutiḥ 
māgadhādivadhādeva duryodhanavadhādapi   
yo ya eva balajyeṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyeṣu sa uttamaḥ 
aṅgaṃ cedviṣṇukāryeṣu tadbhaktyaiva na cānyathā   
balaṃ naisargikaṃ taccedvarāstrādestadanyathā 
anyāveśanimittaṃ cedbalamanyātmakaṃ hi tat   
deveṣu balināmeva bhaktijñāne na cānyathā 
sa eva ca priyo viṣṇornānyathā tu kathañcana   
tasmādyo yo balajyeṣṭhaḥ sa guṇajyeṣṭha eva ca 
balaṃ hi kṣatriye vyaktaṃ j ñāyate sthūladṛṣṭibhiḥ   
j ñānādayo guṇā yasmājjñāyante sūkṣmadṛṣṭibhiḥ 
tasmādyatra balaṃ tatra vijñātavyā guṇāḥ pare   
deveṣveva na cānyeṣu vāsudevapratīpataḥ 
 Mahā  
xvikṣatrādanyeṣvapi balaṃ pramāṇaṃ yatra keśavaḥ 
pravṛtto duṣṭanidhane jñānakārye tathaiva ca   
anyatra brāhmaṇānāṃ tu pramāṇaṃ j ñānameva hi 
kṣatriyāṇāṃ balaṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ viṣṇukāryatā   
kṛṣṇarāmādirūpeṣu balakāryo janārdanaḥ 
dattavyāsādirūpeṣu jñānakāryastathā prabhuḥ   
matsyakūrmavarāhāṇsca siṃ havāmanabhārgavāḥ 
rāghavaḥ kṛṣṇabuddhau ca kṛṣṇadvaipāyanastathā   
kapilo datta ṛṣabhau śiṃ śumāro ruceḥ sutaḥ 
nārāyaṇo hariḥ kṛṣṇastāpaso manureva ca   
mahidāsastathā haṃ saḥ strīrūpo hayaśīrṣavān 
tathaiva vaḍavāvaktraḥ kalkī dhanvantariḥ prabhuḥ   
ityādyāḥ kevalo viṣṇurnaiṣāṃ bhedaḥ kathañcana 
na viśeṣo guṇaiḥ sarvairbalajñānādibhiḥ kvacit   
śrībrahmarudraśeṣāṇsca vīndrendrau kāma eva ca 
kāmaputro'niruddhaśca sūryaścandro bṛhaspatiḥ   
dharma eṣāṃ tathā bhāryā dakṣādyā manavastathā 
manuputrāṇsca ṛṣayo nāradaḥ parvatastathā   
kaśyapaḥ sanakādyāṇsca vahnyādyāṇscaiva devatāḥ 
bharataḥ kārtavīryaśca vainyādyāṇscakravartinaḥ   
gayaśca lakṣmaṇādyāṇsca trayo rohiṇinandanaḥ 
pradyumno raukmiṇeyaśca tatputraścāniruddhakaḥ   
naraḥ phalguna ityādyā viśeṣāveśino hareḥ 
vāli sāmbādayaścaiva kiñcidāveśino hareḥ   
xviitasmādbalapravṛttasya rāmakṛṣṇātmano hareḥ 
antaraṅgaṃ hanūmāṃ śca bhīmastatkāryasādhakau   
brahmātmako yato vāyuḥ padaṃ brāhmamagāt purā 
vāyoranyasya na brāhmaṃ padaṃ tasmāt sa eva saḥ   
yatra rūpaṃ tatra guṇāḥ bhaktyādyāstrīṣu nityaśaḥ 
rūpaṃ hi sthūladṛṣṭīnāṃ dṛśyaṃ vyaktaṃ tato hi tat   
prāyo vettuṃ na śakyante bhaktyādyāstrīṣu yat tataḥ 
yāsāṃ rūpaṃ guṇāstāsāṃ bhaktyādyā iti niścayaḥ   
tacca naisargikaṃ rūpaṃ dvātriṃ śallakṣaṇairyutam 
nālakṣaṇaṃ vapurmātraṃ guṇahetuḥ kathañcana   
āsurīṇāṃ varādestu vapurmātraṃ bhaviṣyati 
na lakṣaṇānyatastāsāṃ naiva bhaktiḥ kathañcana   
tasmād rūpaguṇodārā jānakī rugmiṇī tathā 
satyabhāmetyādirūpā ṇsrīḥ sarvaparamā matā   
tataḥ paścād draupadī ca sarvābhyo rūpato varā 
bhūbhārakṣapaṇe sākṣādaṅgaṃ bhīmavadīśituḥ   
hantā ca vairahetuśca bhīmaḥ pāpajanasya tu 
draupadī vairahetuḥ sā tasmād bhīmādanantarā   
baladevastataḥ paścāt tataḥ paścācca phalgunaḥ 
narāveśādanyathā tu drauṇiḥ paścāt tato'pare   
rāmavajjāmbavatyādyāḥ ṣaṭtato revatī tathā 
lakṣmaṇo hanumatpaścāt tato bharatavālinau 
śatrughnastu tataḥ paścāt sugrīvādyāstato'varāḥ   
xviiirāmakāryaṃ tu yaiḥ samyak svayogyaṃ na kṛtaṃ purā 
taiḥ pūritaṃ tat kṛṣṇāya bībhatsvādyaiḥ samantataḥ   
adhikaṃ yaiḥ kṛtaṃ tatra tairūnaṃ kṛtamatra tat 
karṇādyairadhikaṃ yaistu prādurbhāvadvaye kṛtam 
vividādyairhi taiḥ paścād vipratīpaṃ kṛtaṃ hareḥ   
prādurbhāvadvaye hyasmin sarveṣāṃ nirṇayaḥ kṛtaḥ 
naitayorakṛtaṃ kiñcicchubhaṃ vā yadi vā'śubham 
anyatra pūryate kvāpi tasmādatraiva nirṇayaḥ   
paścāttanatvāt kṛṣṇasya vaiśeṣyāt tatra nirṇayaḥ 
prādurbhāvamimaṃ yasmād gṛhītvā bhārataṃ kṛtam   
uktā rāmakathā'pyasmin mārkaṇḍeyasamāsyayā 
tasmād yad bhārate noktaṃ taddhi naivāsti kutracit 
atroktaṃ sarvaśāstreṣu nahi samyagudāhṛtam   
ityādi kathitaṃ sarvaṃ brahmāṇḍe hariṇā svayam 
mārkaṇḍeye'pi kathitaṃ bhāratasya praśaṃ sanam   
devatānāṃ yathā vyāso dvipadāṃ brāhmaṇo varaḥ 
āyudhānāṃ yathā vajramoṣadhīnāṃ yathā yavāḥ 
tathaiva sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ mahābhāratamuttamam   
vāyuprokte'pi tat proktaṃ bhāratasya praśaṃ sanam  
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ vyāsaṃ viddhi nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum 
ko hyanyaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣānmahābhāratakṛd bhavet   
evaṃ hi sarvaśāstreṣu pṛthak pṛthagudīritam 
ukto'rthaḥ sarva evāyaṃ māhātmyakramapūrvakaḥ

kṛṣṇo vanyairijyate sammṛśānaiḥ kṛṣṇo muktairijyate vītamohaiḥ    
sṛṣṭā brahmādayo devā nihatā yena dānavāḥ 
tasmai devādidevāya namaste śārṅgadhāriṇe

utpattirdaityānāmapi yasmāt sammitā viśeṣo'yam

xxtamimameva surāsurasañcaye harikṛtaṃ praviśeṣamudīkṣitum 
prativibhajya ca bhīmasuyodhanau svaparapakṣabhidā kathitā kathā   
namo bhagavate tasmai vyāsāyāmitatejase 
yasya prasādād vakṣyāmi nārāyaṇakathāmimām   
vāsudevastu bhagavān kīrtito'tra sanātanaḥ 
pratibimbamivā'darśe yaṃ paśyantyātmani sthitam   
nāsti nārāyaṇasamaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati 
etena satyavākyena sarvārthān sādhayāmyaham   
ādyantayorityavadat sa yasmād vyāsātmako viṣṇurudāraśaktiḥ 
tasmāt samastā harisadguṇānāṃ nirṇītaye bhāratagā kathaiṣā   
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyamuddhṛtya bhujamucyate 
vedaśāstrāt paraṃ nāsti na daivaṃ keśavāt param   
āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ 
idamekaṃ suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā   
smartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇurvismartavyo na jātucit 
sarve vidhiniṣedhāḥ syuretayoreva kiṅkarāḥ    
ko hi taṃ vedituṃ śakto yo na syāt tadvidho'paraḥ 
tadvidhaścāparo nāsti tasmāt taṃ veda saḥ svayam   
ko hi taṃ vedituṃ śakto nārāyaṇamanāmayam 
ṛte satyavatīsūnoḥ kṛṣṇād vā devakīsutāt   
aprameyo'niyojyaśca svayaṃ kāmagamo vaśī 
modatyeṣa sadā bhūtairbālaḥ krīḍanakairiva   
na pramātuṃ mahābāhuḥ śakyo'yaṃ madhusūdanaḥ 
xxiparamāt parametasmād viśvarūpānna vidyate   
vasudevasuto nāyaṃ nāyaṃ garbhe'vasat prabhuḥ 
nāyaṃ daśarathājjāto na cāpi jamadagnitaḥ   
j āyate naiva kutrāpi mriyate kuta eva tu 
na vedhyo muhyate nāyaṃ baddhyate naiva kenacit 
kuto duḥkhaṃ svatantrasya nityānandaikarūpiṇaḥ   
īśannapi hi deveśaḥ sarvasya jagato hariḥ 
karmāṇi kurute nityaṃ kīnāṇsa iva durbalaḥ   
nā'tmānaṃ veda mugdho'yaṃ duḥkhī sīt āṃ ca mārgate 
baddhaḥ śakrajitetyādi līlaiṣā'suramohinī   
muhyate śastrapātena bhinnatvagrudhirasravaḥ 
ajānan pṛcchati smānyāṃ stanuṃ tyaktvā divaṃ gataḥ   
ityādyasuramohāya darśayāmāsa nāṭyavat 
avidyamānameveśaḥ kuhakaṃ tad viduḥ surāḥ   
prādurbhāvā hareḥ sarve naiva prakṛtidehinaḥ 
nirdoṣā guṇasampūrṇā darśayantyanyathaiva tu   
duṣṭānāṃ mohanārthāya satāmapi tu kutracit 
yathāyogyaphalaprāptyai līlaiṣā paramātmanaḥ    
jñānaṃ te'haṃ savijñānamidaṃ vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ 
yajjñātvā neha bhūyo'nyajjñātavyamavaśiṣyate

 Bha Gī 
xxiiavajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanumāṇsritam 
moghāṇsā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ 
rākṣasīmāsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohanīṃ śritāḥ     
mahātmānastu māṃ pārtha daivīṃ prakṛtimāṇsritāḥ 
bhajantyananyamanaso jñātvā bhūtādimavyayam   
pitā'si lokasya carācarasya tvamasya pūjyaśca gururgarīyān 
na tvatsamo'styabhyadhikaḥ kuto'nyo lokatraye'pyapratimaprabhāva   
paraṃ bhūyaḥ pravakṣyāmi j ñānānāṃ j ñānamuttamam 
yajjñātvā munayaḥ sarve parāṃ siddhimito gatāḥ     
mamayonirmahad brahma tasmin garbhaṃ dadhāmyaham 
sambhavaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tato bhavati bhārata   
dvāvimau puruṣau loke kṣaraścākṣara eva ca 
kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭastho'kṣara ucyate   
uttamaḥ puruṣastvanyaḥ paramātmetyudāhṛtaḥ 
yo lokatrayamāviśya bibhartyavyaya īśvaraḥ   
yasmāt kṣaramatīto'hamakṣarādapi cottamaḥ 
ato'smi loke vede ca prathitaḥ puruṣottamaḥ   
yo māmevamasammūḍho jānāti puruṣottamam

xxiiietad buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaśca bhārata   
dvau bhūtasargau loke'smin daiva āsura eva ca 
daivo vistaraśaḥ prokta āsuraṃ pārtha me śṛṇu    
asatyamapratiṣṭhaṃ te jagadāhuranīśvaram 
īśvaro'hamahaṃ bhogī siddho'haṃ balavān sukhī    
māmātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto'bhyasūyakāḥ   
tānahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃ sāreṣu narādhamān 
kṣipāmyajasramaśubhānāsurīṣveva yoniṣu   
āsurīṃ yonimāpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani 
māmaprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yāntyadhamāṃ gatim   
sarvabhūteṣu yenaikaṃ bhāvamavyayamīkṣate 
avibhaktaṃ vibhakteṣu tajjñānaṃ viddhi sātvikam   
sarvaguhyatamaṃ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu me paramaṃ vacaḥ 
iṣṭo'si me dṛḍhamiti tato vakṣyāmi te hitam   
manmanā bhava madbhakto madyājī māṃ namaskuru 
māmevaiṣyasi satyaṃ te pratijāne priyo'si me   
pañcarātrasya kṛtsnasya vaktā nārāyaṇaḥ svayam 
sarveṣveteṣu rājendra jñāneṣvetad viśiṣyate

xxivjñāneṣveteṣu rājendra sāṅkhyapāṇsupatādiṣu 
yathāyogaṃ yathānyāyaṃ niṣṭhā nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ     
pañcarātravido mukhyā yathākramaparā nṛpa 
ekāntabhāvopagatā vāsudevaṃ viśanti te   
janamejaya uvāca
bahavaḥ puruṣā brahmannutāho eka eva tu 
ko hyatra puruṣaṇsreṣṭhastaṃ bhavān vaktumarhati   
vaiśampāyana uvāca 
naitadicchanti puruṣamekaṃ kurukulodvaha 
bahūnāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ hi yathaikā yonirucyate 
tathā taṃ puruṣaṃ viśvamākhyāsyāmi guṇādhikam   
āha brahmaitamevārthaṃ mahādevāya pṛcchate 
tasyaikasya mamatvaṃ hi sa caikaḥ puruṣo virāṭ   
ahaṃ brahmā cā'dya īśaḥ prajānāṃ
tasmājjātastvaṃ ca mattaḥ prasūtaḥ 
matto jagat sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca
sarve vedā sarahasyāṇsca putra   
tathaiva bhīmavacanaṃ dharmajaṃ pratyudīritam 
brahmeśānādibhiḥ sarvaiḥ sametairyadguṇāṃ śakaḥ 
nāvasāyayituṃ śakyo vyācakṣāṇaiśca sarvadā

xxvsa eṣa bhagavān kṛṣṇo naiva kevalamānuṣaḥ 
yasya prasādajo brahmā rudraśca krodhasambhavaḥ    
vacanaṃ caiva kṛṣṇasya jyeṣṭhaṃ kuntīsutaṃ prati 
rudraṃ samāṇsritā devā rudro brahmāṇamāṇsritaḥ 
brahmā māmāṇsrito nityaṃ nāhaṃ kiñcidupāṇsritaḥ   
yathāśritāni jyotīṃ ṣi jyotiḥ śreṣṭhaṃ divākaram 
evaṃ muktagaṇāḥ sarve vāsudevamupāṇsritāḥ    
bhaviṣyatparvagaṃ cāpi vaco vyāsasya sādaram 
vāsudevasya mahimā bhārate nirṇayoditaḥ   
tadarthāstu kathāḥ sarvā nānyārthaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ 
tatpratīpaṃ tu yad dṛśyenna tanmama manīṣitam   
bhāṣāstu trividhāstatra mayā vai sampradarśitāḥ 
ukto yo mahimā viṣṇoḥ sa tūkto hi samādhinā   
śaivadarśanamālambya kvacicchaivī kathoditā 
samādhibhāṣayoktaṃ yat tat sarvaṃ grāhyameva hi   
aviruddhaṃ samādhestu darśanoktaṃ ca gṛhyate 
ādyantayorviruddhaṃ yad darśanaṃ tadudāhṛtam   
darśanāntarasiddhaṃ ca guhyabhāṣā'nyathā bhavet 
tasmād viṣṇorhi mahimā bhāratokto yathārthataḥ   
tasyāṅgaṃ prathamaṃ vāyuḥ prādurbhāvatrayānvitaḥ 
prathamo hanumān nāma dvitīyo bhīma eva ca 
pūrṇaprajñastṛtīyastu bhagavatkāryasādhakaḥ   
tretādyeṣu yugeṣveṣa sambhūtaḥ keśavājñayā 
ekaikaśastriṣu pṛthag dvitīyāṅgaṃ sarasvatī   
xxviśaṃ rūpe tu ratervāyau śrīrityeva ca kīrtyate 
saiva ca draupadī nāma kāl  ī candreti cocyate   
tṛtīyāṅgaṃ hareḥ śeṣaḥ prādurbhāvasamanvitaḥ 
prādurbhāvā naraścaiva lakṣmaṇo bala eva ca   
rudrātmakatvāccheṣasya śuko drauṇiśca tattanū 
indre narāṃ śasampattyā pārtho'pīṣat tadātmakaḥ   
pradyumnādyāstato viṣṇoraṅgabhūtāḥ krameṇa tu
caritaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ tad viṣṇūdrekāya kathyate   
tathā bhāgavate'pyuktaṃ hanūmadvacanaṃ param 
martyāvatārastviha martyaśikṣaṇaṃ rakṣovadhāyaiva na kevalaṃ vibhoḥ 
kuto'sya hi syū ramataḥ sva ātman sīt ākṛt āni vyasanānīśvarasya   
na vai sa ātmā'tmavatāmadhīśvaro bhuṅkte hi duḥkhaṃ bhagavān vāsudevaḥ 
na strīkṛtaṃ kaśmalamaśnuvīta na lakṣmaṇaṃ cāpi jahāti karhicit   
yatpādapaṅkajaparāganiṣevakāṇāṃ duḥkhāni sarvāṇi layaṃ prayānti 
sa brahmavandyacaraṇo janamohanāya strīsa' ngināmiti ratiṃ prathayaṃ ścacāra   
kvacicchivaṃ kvacidṛṣīn kvacid devān kvacinnarān 
namatyarcayati stauti varānarthayate'pi ca   
li ṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati vṛṇotyasurato varān 
sarveśvaraḥ svatantro'pi sarvaśaktiśca sarvadā 
sarvajño'pi vimohāya janānāṃ puruṣottamaḥ    
tasmād yo mahimā viṣṇoḥ sarvaśāstroditaḥ sa hi 
nānyadityeṣa ṇsāstrāṇāṃ nirṇayaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ

xxviibhāratārthastridhā proktaḥ svayaṃ bhagavataiva hi   
manvādi kecid bruvate hyāstīkādi tathā pare 
tathoparicarādyanye bhārataṃ paricakṣate  
sakṛṣṇān pāṇḍavān gṛhya yo'yamarthaḥ pravartate 
prātilomyādivaicitryāt tamāstīkaṃ pracakṣate   
dharmo bhaktyādidaśakaḥ śrutādiḥ śīlavainayau 
sabrahmakāstu te yatra manvādiṃ taṃ vidurbudhāḥ   
nārāyaṇasya nāmāni sarvāṇi vacanāni tu 
tatsāmarthyābhidhāyīni tamauparicaraṃ viduḥ   
bhaktirjñānaṃ savairāgyaṃ prajñā medhā dhṛtiḥ sthitiḥ 
yogaḥ prāṇo balaṃ caiva vṛkodara iti smṛtaḥ   
etaddaśātmako vāyustasmād bhīmastadātmakaḥ 
sarvavidyā draupadī tu yasmāt saiva sarasvatī   
ajñānādisvarūpastu kalirduryodhanaḥ smṛtaḥ 
viparītaṃ tu yajjñānaṃ duḥ śāsana itīritaḥ   
nāstikyaṃ śakunirnāma sarvadoṣātmakāḥ pare 
dhārtarāṣṭrāstvahaṅkāro drauṇī rudrātmako yataḥ   
droṇādyā indriyāṇyeva pāpānyanye tu sainikāḥ 
pāṇḍaveyāṇsca puṇyāni teṣāṃ viṣṇurniyojakaḥ   
evamadhyātmaniṣṭhaṃ hi bhārataṃ sarvamucyate 
durvijñeyamataḥ sarvairbhārataṃ tu surairapi   
svayaṃ vyāso hi tad veda brahmā vā tatprasādataḥ

xxviiitathā'pi viṣṇuparatā bhārate sārasaṅgrahaḥ    
ityādivyāsavākyaistu viṣṇūtkarṣo'vagamyate 
vāyvādīnāṃ kramaścaiva tadvākyaireva cintyate   
vāyurhi brahmatāmeti tasmād brahmaiva sa smṛtaḥ 
na brahmasadṛśaḥ kaścicchivādiṣu kathañcana   
jñāne virāge haribhaktibhāve dhṛtisthitiprāṇabaleṣu yoge 
buddhau ca nānyo hanumatsamānaḥ pumān kadācit kva ca kaścanaiva   
bal  itthā tad vapuṣe dhāyi darśataṃ devasya bhargaḥ sahaso yato jani 
yadīm upahvarate sādhate matir ṛtasya dhenā anayanta sasrutaḥ   
pṛkṣo vapuḥ pitumān nitya āṇsaye dvitīyam ā saptaśivāsu mātṛṣu 
tṛtīyam asya vṛṣbhasya dohase daśapramatiṃ janayanta yoṣaṇaḥ   
niryad īm budhnān mahiṣasya varpasa īśānāsaḥ śavasā kranta sūrayaḥ 
yad īm anu pradivo madhva ādhave guhāsantam mātariśvā mathāyati   
pra yat pituḥ paramān nīyate paryā pṛkṣudho vīrudho daṃ su rohati 
ubhā yad asya januṣaṃ yad invata ād id yaviṣṭho abhavad ghṛṇā ṇsuciḥ   
ād in mātṛrāviśad yāsvā ṇsucir ahiṃ syamāna urviyā vivāvṛdhe 
anuyat pūrvā aruhat sanājuvo ni navyaśīṣvavarāsu dhāvate   
aśvamedhaḥ kratuśreṣṭho jyotiḥ śreṣṭho divākaraḥ 
brāhmaṇo dvipadāṃ śreṣṭho devaśreṣṭhastu mārutaḥ    
balamindrasya giriśo giriśasya balaṃ marut 
balaṃ tasya hariḥ sākṣānna harerbalamanyataḥ    
vāyurbhīmo bhīmanādo mahaujāḥ sarveṣāṃ ca prāṇināṃ prāṇabhūtaḥ

xxixanāvṛttirdehināṃ dehapāte tasmād vāyurdevadevo viśiṣṭaḥ    
tattvajñāne viṣṇubhaktau dhairye sthairye parākrame 
vege ca lāghave caiva pralāpasya ca varjane   
bhīmasenasamo nāsti senayorubhayorapi 
pāṇḍitye ca paṭutve ca śūratve ca bale'pi ca   
tathā yudhiṣṭhireṇāpi bhīmaṃ prati samīritam 
dharmaścārthaśca kāmaśca mokṣaṇscaiva yaśo dhruvam 
tvayyāyattamidaṃ sarvaṃ sarvalokasya bhārata   
virāṭaparvagaṃ cāpi vaco duryodhanasya hi  
vīrāṇāṃ śāstraviduṣāṃ kṛtināṃ tattvanirṇaye 
sattve bāhubale dhairye prāṇe ṇsārīrasambhave   
sāmprataṃ mānuṣe loke sadaityanararākṣase 
catvāraḥ prāṇināṃ śreṣṭhāḥ sampūrṇabalapauruṣāḥ   
bhīmaśca balabhadraśca madrarājaśca vīryavān 
caturthaḥ kīcakasteṣāṃ pañcamaṃ nānuśuśrumaḥ 
anyonyānantarabalāḥ kramādeva prakīrtitāḥ    
vacanaṃ vāsudevasya tathodyogagataṃ param 
yat kiñcā'tmani kalyāṇaṃ sambhāvayasi pāṇḍava 
sahasraguṇamapyetat tvayi sambhāvayāmyaham   
yādṛśe ca kule jātaḥ sarvarājābhipūjite 
 vīrāṇāṃ śāstraviduṣām
nāsti nārāyaṇasamam ityādi mahābhāratādyuktāni
bhagavatpādairudāhṛtāni mudritapustakeṣu anupalabhyatve'pi prācīnakośeṣu
prāyaśaḥ dṛṣyante 
xxxyādṛśāni ca karmāṇi bhīma tvamasi tādṛśaḥ    
asmin yuddhe bhīmasena tvayi bhāraḥ samāhitaḥ 
dhūrarjunena voḍhavyā voḍhavya itaro janaḥ   
uktaṃ purāṇe brahmāṇḍe brahmaṇā nāradāya ca   
yasyāḥ prasādāt paramaṃ vidanti śeṣaḥ suparṇo giriśaḥ surendraḥ 
mātā ca yaiṣāṃ prathamaiva bhāratī sā draupadī nāma babhūva bhūmau   
yā mārutād garbhamadhatta pūrvaṃ śeṣaṃ suparṇaṃ girīśaṃ surendram 
caturmukhābhāṃ ścaturaḥ kumārān sā draupadī nāma babhūva bhūmau   
yasyādhiko bale nāsti bhīmasenamṛte kvacit 
na vijñāne na ca jñāna eṣa rāmaḥ sa lāṅgalī   
yasya na pratiyoddhā'sti bhīmamekamṛte kvacit 
anviṣyāpi trilokeṣu sa eṣa musalāyudhaḥ    
tathā yudhiṣṭhireṇaiva bhīmāya samudīritam 
anujñāto rauhiṇeyāt tvayā caivāparājita 
sarvavidyāsu bībhatsuḥ kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā   
anveṣa rauhiṇeyaṃ ca tvāṃ ca bhīmāparājitam 
vīrye śaurye'pi vā nānyastṛtīyaḥ phalgunādṛte   
tathaiva draupadīvākyaṃ vāsudevaṃ pratīritam 
adhijyamapi yat kartuṃ śakyate naiva gāṇḍivam 
anyatra bhīmapārthābhyāṃ bhavataśca janārdana   
tathaivānyatra vacanaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyaneritam

xxxidvāveva puruṣau loke vāsudevādanantarau 
bhīmastu prathamastatra dvitīyo drauṇireva ca   
akṣayāviṣudhī divye dhvajo vānaralakṣaṇaḥ 
gāṇḍīvaṃ dhanuṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tena drauṇervaro'rjunaḥ    
ityādyanantavākyāni santyevārthe vivakṣite 
kānicid darśitānyatra diṇmātrapratipattaye   
tasmāduktakrameṇaiva puruṣottamatā hareḥ 
anaupacārikī siddhā brahmatā ca vinirṇayāt   
pūrṇaprajñakṛteyaṃ saṅkṣepāduddhṛtiḥ suvākyānām 
śrīmadbhāratagānāṃ viṣṇoḥ pūrṇatvanirṇayāyaiva   
sa prīyatāṃ paratamaḥ paramādanantaḥ santārakaḥ satatasaṃ sṛtidustarārṇāt 
yatpādapadmamakarandajuṣo hipārthāḥ svārājyamāpurubhayatra sadā vinodāt   
iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite
śrīmahābhāratatātparyanirṇaye

atha tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ
Oṃ  jayatyajo'khaṇḍaguṇorumaṇḍalaḥ sadodito jñānamarīcimālī 
svabhaktahārdoccatamonihantā vyāsāvatāro harirātmabhāskaraḥ   
jayatyajo'kṣīṇasukhātmabimbaḥ svaiśvaryakāntipratataḥ sadoditaḥ 
svabhaktasantāpaduriṣṭahantā rāmāvatāro harirīśacandramāḥ   
jayatyasaṅkhyorubalāmbupūro guṇoccaratnākara ātmavaibhavaḥ 
sadā sadātmajñanadībhirāpyaḥ kṛṣṇāvatāro harirekasāgaraḥ   
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam 
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīraye  
jayo nāmetihāso'yaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyaneritaḥ 
vāyurnarottamo nāma devīti śrīrudīritā   
nārāyaṇo vyāsa iti vācyavaktṛsvarūpakaḥ 
ekaḥ sa bhagavānuktaḥ sādhakeśo narottamaḥ   
upasādhako naraścokto devī bhāgyātmikā nṛṇām 
sarasvatī vākyarūpā tasmānnamyā hi te'khilāḥ 
kṛṣṇau satyā bhīmapārthau kṛṣṇetyuktā hibhārate   
sarvasya nirṇayasuvākyasamuddhṛtī tusvādhyāyayorharipadasmaraṇena kṛtvā 
ānandatīrthavaranāmavatī tṛtīyā bhaumī tanurmaruta āha kathāḥ parasya   
vyūḍhaścaturdhā bhagavān sa eko māyāṃ śriyaṃ sṛṣṭividhitsayā'ra 
rūpeṇa pūrveṇa savāsudevanāmnā viriñcaṃ suṣuve ca sā'taḥ   
saṅkarṣaṇāccāpi jayātanūjo babhūva sākṣād balasaṃ vidātmā 
vāyurya evātha viriñcanāmā bhaviṣya ādyo na parastato hi   
 Mahā Ādi  
xxxiiisūtraṃ sa vāyuḥ puruṣo viriñcaḥ pradyumnataścātha kṛtau striyau dve 
prajajñaturyamal  e tatra pūrvā pradhānasañjñā prakṛtirjanitrī   
śraddhā dvitīyā'tha tayośca yogo babhūva puṃ saiva ca sūtranāmnā 
harerniyogādatha samprasūtau śeṣaḥ suparṇaṇsca tayoḥ sahaiva   
śeṣastayoreva hi jīvanāmā kālātmakaḥ so'tha suparṇa āsīt 
tau vāhanaṃ śayanaṃ caiva viṣṇoḥ kālā jayādyāṇsca tata prasūtāḥ   
kālā jayādyā api viṣṇupārṣadā yasmādaṇḍāt parataḥ samprasūtāḥ 
nīcāḥ surebhyastata eva te'khilā viṣvakseno vāyujaḥ khena tulyaḥ   
vyūhāt tṛtīyāt punareva viṣṇordevāṃ ścaturvarṇagatān samastān 
saṅgṛhya bīj ātmatayā'niruddho nyadhatta śāntyāṃ triguṇātmikāyām   
tato mahattattvatanurviriñcaḥ sthūlātmanaivājani vāk ca devī 
tasyāmahaṅkāratanuṃ sa rudraṃ sasarja buddhiṃ ca tadarddhadehām   
buddhyāmumāyāṃ sa śivastrirūpo manaśca vaikārikadevasaṅghān 
daśendriyāṇyeva ca taijasāni krameṇa khādīn viṣayaiśca sārddham   
puṃ saḥ prakṛtyāṃ ca punarviriñcācchivo'tha tasmādakhilāḥ sureśāḥ 
j ātāḥ saśakrāḥ punareva sūtrācchraddhā sutānāpa surapravīrān 
śeṣaṃ śivaṃ cendramathendrataśca sarve surā yajñagaṇāṇsca jātāḥ   
punaśca māyā trividhā babhūva sattvādirūpairatha vāsudevāt 
sattvātmikāyāṃ sa babhūva tasmāt sa viṣṇunāmaiva nirantaro'pi 
rajastanau caiva viriñca āsīt tamastanau śarva iti trayo'smāt   
ete hi devāḥ punaraṇḍasṛṣṭāvaśaknuvanto harimetya tuṣṭuvuḥ 
tvaṃ no jagaccitravicitrasarganissīmaśaktiḥ kuru sanniketam   
iti stutastaiḥ puruṣottamo'sau sa viṣṇunāmā ṇsriyamāpa sṛṣṭaye 
suṣāva saivāṇḍamadhokṣajasya śuṣmaṃ hiraṇyātmakamambumadhye   
xxxivtasmin praviṣṭā hariṇaiva sārddhaṃ sarve surāstasya babhūva nābheḥ 
lokātmakaṃ padmamamuṣya madhye punarviriñco'jani sadguṇātmā   
tasmāt punaḥ sarvasurāḥ prasūtāste jānamānā api nirṇayāya 
nissṛtya kāyāduta padmayoneḥ samprāviśan kramaśo mārutāntāḥ   
papāta vāyorgamanāccharīraṃ tasyaiva cā'veśata utthitaṃ punaḥ 
tasmāt sa eko vibudhapradhāna ityāṇsritā devagaṇāstameva 
harerviriñcasya ca madhyasaṃ sthitestadanyadevādhipatiḥ sa mārutaḥ   
tato viriñco bhuvanāni sapta sasaptakānyāṇsu cakāra so'bjāt 
tasmācca devā ṛṣayaḥ punaśca vaikārikādyāḥ saśivā babhūvuḥ   
agre śivo'hambhava eva buddherumā manojau saha śakrakāmau 
gururmanurdakṣa utāniruddhaḥ sahaiva paścānmanasaḥ prasūtāḥ   
cakṣuḥ śrutibhyāṃ sparśāt sahaiva raviḥ śaśī dharma ime prasūtāḥ 
jihvābhavo vāripatirnasośca nāsatyadasrau kramaśaḥ prasūtāḥ   
tataḥ sanādyāṇsca marīcimukhyā devāṇsca sarve kramaśaḥ prasūtāḥ

Oṃ  athābhyavardhaṃ ścaturāḥ kumārā nṛpasya gehe puruṣottamādyāḥ

saṃ svinnagātrāḥ parivṛttanetrā daśānanādyāḥ patitā vimūrchitāḥ 
tathā'pi māṃ dharṣayituṃ na śekuḥ sutākṛte te vacanāṃ svayambhuvaḥ

Oṃ  utthāpya cainamaravindadalāyatākṣaṇscakrāṅkitena varadena karāmbujena 
kṛtvā ca saṃ vidamanena nuto'sya cāṃ saṃ prītyā'ruroha sa hasan saha lakṣmaṇena   
āropya cāṃ sayugal  aṃ bhagavantamenaṃ tasyānujaṃ ca hanumān prayayau kapīndram 
sakhyaṃ cakāra hutabhukpramukhe ca tasya rāmeṇa ṇsāṇsvatanijārtihareṇa ṇsīghram   
śrutvā'sya duḥkhamatha devavaraḥ pratijñāṃ cakre sa vālinidhanāya harīśvaro'pi 
sīt ānumārgaṇakṛte'tha sa vālinaiva kṣiptāṃ hi dundubhitanuṃ samadarśayacca   
vīkṣyaiva tāṃ nipatitāmatha rāmadevaḥ so'ṅguṣṭhamātracalanādatilīlayaiva 
samprāsya yojanaśate'tha tayaiva corvīṃ sarvāṃ vidārya ditijānahanad rasāsthān   
śarvaprasādajabalād ditijānavadhyān sarvān nihatya kuṇapena punaśca sakhyā 
bhītena vālibalataḥ kathitaḥ sma sapta sālān pradarśya ditijān sudṛḍhāṃ śca vajrāt   
ekaikameṣu sa vikampayituṃ samarthaḥ patrāṇi loptumapi tūtsahate na śaktaḥ 
viṣvak sthitān yadi bhavān pratibhetsyatīmānekeṣuṇā tarhi vālivadhe samarthaḥ   
jetuṃ caturguṇabalo hi pumān prabhuḥ syāddhantuṃ śatādhikabalo'tibalaṃ suśaktaḥ 
tasmādimān harihayātmajabāhvalopyapatrān vibhidya mama saṃ śayamāṇsu bhindhi   
śrutvā'sya vākyamavamṛśya diteḥ sutāṃ stān dhāturvarādakhilapumbhirabhedyarūpān 
brahmatvamāptumacalaṃ tapasi pravṛtt ānekeṣuṇā sapadi tān pravibheda rāmaḥ   
sandhāya kārmukavare niśite tu bāṇe'thā'kṛṣya dakṣiṇabhujena tadā pramukte 
rāmeṇa satvaramanantabalena sarve cūrṇīkṛt āḥ sapadi te taravo raveṇa   
bhittvā catān sagirikuṃ bhagavatpramuktaḥ pātāl  asaptakamathātra ca ye tvavadhyāḥ 
nāmnā'surāḥ kumudino'bjajavākyarakṣāḥ sarvāṃ śca tānadahadāṇsu śaraḥ sa ekaḥ   
naitad vicitramamitorubalasya viṣṇoryatpreraṇāt sapavanasya bhavet pravṛttiḥ 
lokasya saprakṛtikasya sarudrakāla karmādikasya tadapīdamananyasādhyam   
liidṛṣṭvā balaṃ bhagavato'tha harīśvaro'sāvagre nidhāya tamayāt puramagrajasya 
āṇsrutya rāvamanujasya bilāt sa cā'gādabhyenamāṇsu dayitāprativārito'pi   
tanmuṣṭibhiḥ pratihataḥ prayayāvaśaktaḥ sugrīva āṇsu raghupo'pi hi dharmamīkṣan 
nainaṃ jaghāna viditākhilalokaceṣṭo'pyenaṃ sa āha yudhi vāṃ na mayā viviktau   
saubhrātrameṣa yadi vāñchati vālinaiva nāhaṃ nirāgasamathāgrajaniṃ haniṣye 
dīrghaḥ sahodaragato na bhaveddhi kopo dīrgho'pi kāraṇamṛte vinivartate ca   
kopaḥ sahodarajane punarantakāle prāyo nivṛttimupagacchati tāpakaśca 
ekasya bhaṅga iti naiva jhaṭityapāstadoṣo nihantumiha yogya iti sma mene   
tasmānna bandhujanage janite virodhe kāryo vadhastadanubandhibhirāṇsvitīha 
dharmaṃ pradarśayitumeva raveḥ sutasya bhāvī na tāpa iti vicca na taṃ jaghāna   
yaḥ prerakaḥ sakalaṣemuṣisantateśca tasyājñatā kuta iheśavarasya viṣṇoḥ 
tenodito'tha sudṛḍhaṃ punarāgatena vajropamaṃ śaramamūmucadindrasūnoḥ   
rāmājñayaiva latayā ravije vibhakte vāyoḥ sutena raghupeṇa ṇsare ca mukte 
śrutvā'sya śabdamatulaṃ hṛdi tena viddha indrātmajo giririvāpatadāṇsu sannaḥ   
bhakto mamaiṣa yadi māmabhipaśyatīha pādau dhruvaṃ mama sameṣyati nirvicāraḥ 
yogyo vadho nahi janasya padānatasya rājyārthinā ravisutena vadho'rthitaśca   
kāryaṃ hyabhīṣṭamapi tat praṇatasya pūrvaṃ śasto vadho na padayoḥ praṇatasya caiva 
tasmādadṛśyatanureva nihanmi śakraputraṃ tvitīha tamadṛṣṭatayā jaghāna   
yaḥ prerakaḥ sakalalokabalasya nityaṃ pūrṇāvyayoccabalavīryatanuḥ svatantraḥ 
kiṃ tasya dṛṣṭipathagasya ca vānaro'yaṃ kartaiśacāpamapi yena purā vibhagnam   
sanne'tha vālini jagāma ca tasya pārśvaṃ prāhainamārdravacasā yadi vāñchasi tvam 
ujjīvayiṣya iti naicchadasau tvadagre ko nāma necchati mṛtiṃ puruṣottameti   
kāryāṇi tasya caramāṇi vidhāya putraṃ tvagre nidhāya ravijaḥ kapirājya āsīt 
liiirāmo'pi tadgirivare caturo'tha māsān dṛṣṭvā ghanāgamamuvāsa salakṣmaṇo'sau   
athātisakte kṣitipe kapīnāṃ pravismṛte rāmakṛtopakāre 
prasahya taṃ buddhimatāṃ variṣṭho rāmāṅghribhakto hanumānuvāca   
na vismṛtiste raghuvaryakārye kāryā kathañcit sa hi no'bhipūjyaḥ 
na cet svayaṃ kartumabhīṣṭamadya te dhruvaṃ balenāpi hi kārayāmi   
sa evamuktvā harirājasannidhau dvīpeṣu saptasvapi vānarān prati 
sammel  anāyā'śugatīn sma vānarān prasthāpayāmāsa samastaśaḥ prabhuḥ   
harīśvarājñāpraṇidhānapūrvakaṃ hanūmatā te prahitā hivānarāḥ 
samastaśailadrumaṣaṇḍasaṃ sthitān harīn samādāya tadā'bhijagmuḥ   
tadaiva rāmo'pi hi bhogasaktaṃ pramattamālakṣya kapīśvaraṃ prabhuḥ 
jagāda saumitrimidaṃ vaco me plavaṅgameśāya vadā'śu yāhi   
yadi pramatto'si madīyakārye nayāmyahaṃ tvendrasutasya mārgam 
prāyaḥ svakārye pratipādite hi madoddhatā na pratikartumīśate   
itīḍyarāmeṇa samīrite tadā yayau sabāṇaḥ sadhanuḥ sa lakṣmaṇaḥ 
dṛṣṭvaiva taṃ tena sahaiva tāpanirbhayād yayau rāmapadāntikaṃ tvaran   
hanūmataḥ sādhuvacobhirāṇsu prasannacetasyadhipe kapīnām 
samāgate sarvaharipravīraiḥ sahaiva taṃ vīkṣya nananda rāghavaḥ   
sasambhramaṃ taṃ patitaṃ padābjayostvaran samutthāpya samāṇsliṣat prabhuḥ 
sa copaviṣṭo jagadīśasannidhau tadājñayaivā'diśadāṇsu vānarān   
samastadikṣu prahiteṣu tena prabhurhanūmantamidaṃ babhāṣe 
na kaścidīśastvadṛte'sti sādhane samastakāryapravarasya me'sya   
atastvameva pratiyāhi dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ samādāya madaṅgulīyakam 
itīrito'sau puruṣottamena yayau diśaṃ t āṃ yuvarājayuktaḥ   
livsamastadikṣu pratiyāpitā hi te harīśvarājñāmupadhārya māsataḥ 
samāyayuste'ṅgadajāmbavanmukhāḥ sutena vāyoḥ sahitā nacā'yayuḥ   
samastadurgapravaraṃ durāsadaṃ vimārgatāṃ vindhyagiriṃ mahātmanām 
gataḥ sa kālo harirāḍudīritaḥ samāsadaṃ ścātha bilaṃ mahādbhutam   
kṛtaṃ mayenātivicitramuttamaṃ samīkṣya tat tāra uvāca cāṅgadam 
vayaṃ na yāmo harirājasannidhiṃ vilaṅghito naḥ samayo yato'sya   
durāsado'sāvaticaṇḍaṇsāsano haniṣyati tvāmapi kiṃ madādikān 
agamyametad bilamāpya tat sukhaṃ vasāma sarve kimasāvihā'caret   
na caiva rāmeṇa salakṣmaṇena prayojanaṃ no vanacāriṇāṃ sadā 
na ceha naḥ pīḍayituṃ sa ca kṣamastato mameyaṃ suviniścitā matiḥ   
itīritaṃ mātulavākyamāṇsu sa ādade vālisuto'pi sādaram 
uvāca vākyaṃ ca na no harīśvaraḥ kṣamī bhavellaṅghitaśāsanānām   
rājyārthinā yena hi ghātito'grajo hṛt āṇsca dārāḥ sunṛśaṃ sakena 
sa naḥ kathaṃ rakṣati śāsanātigān nirāṇsrayān durbalakān bale sthitaḥ   
itīrite śakrasutātmajena tatheti hocuḥ saha jāmbavanmukhāḥ 
sarve'pi teṣāmatha caikamatyaṃ dṛṣṭvā hanūmānidamābabhāṣe   
vijñātametaddhi mayā'ṅgadasya rājyāya tārābhihitaṃ hi vākyam 
sādhyaṃ na caitannahi vāyusūnū rāmapratīpaṃ vacanaṃ saheta   
na cāhamākraṣṭumupāyato'pi śakyaḥ kathañcit sakalaiḥ sametaiḥ 
sanmārgato naiva ca rāghavasya durantaśakterbilamapradhṛṣyam   
vaco mamaitad yadi cā'dareṇa grāhyaṃ bhaved vastadatipriyaṃ me 
na ced balādapyanaye pravṛtt ān praśāsya sanmārgagatān karomi   
itīritaṃ tat pavanātmajasya śrutvā'tibhīt ā dhṛtamūkabhāvāḥ 
sarve'nujagmustamathādrimukhyaṃ mahendramāseduragādhabodhāḥ   
lvnirīkṣya te sāgaramapradhṛṣyamapārameyaṃ sahasā viṣaṇṇāḥ 
dṛḍhaṃ nirāṇsāṇsca matiṃ hi dadhruḥ prāyopaveśāya tathā ca cakruḥ   
prāyopaviṣṭāṇsca kathā vadanto rāmasya saṃ sāravimuktidātuḥ 
jaṭāyuṣaḥ pātanamūcuretat sampātināmnaḥ śravaṇaṃ jagāma   
tasyāgrajo'sāvaruṇasya sūnuḥ sūryasya bimbaṃ saha tena yātaḥ 
javaṃ parīkṣannatha taṃ sutaptaṃ guptvā patatrakṣayamāpya cāpatat   
sa dagdhapakṣaḥ savitṛpratāpācchrutvaiva rāmasya kathāṃ sapakṣaḥ 
bhūtvā punaścāpi mṛtiṃ jaṭāyuṣaḥ śuśrāva pṛṣṭvā punareva samyak   
sa rāvaṇasyātha gatiṃ sutoktāṃ nivedya dṛṣṭvā janakātmajākṛtim 
svayaṃ tathā'śokavane niṣaṇṇāmavocadebhyo haripuṅgavebhyaḥ   
tatastu te brahmasutena pṛṣṭā nyavedayannātmabalaṃ pṛthak pṛthak 
daśaiva cā'rabhya daśottarasya kramāt patho yojanato'tiyāne   
sanīlamaindadvividāḥ satārāḥ sarve'pyaśītyāḥ parato na śaktāḥ 
gantuṃ yadā'thā'tmabalaṃ sa jāmbavān jagāda tasmāt punaraṣṭamāṃ śam   
baleryadā viṣṇuravāpa lokāṃ stribhiḥ kramairnandiravaṃ prakurvatā 
tadā mayā bhrāntamidaṃ jagattrayaṃ savedanaṃ j ānu mamā'sa merutaḥ   
ato javo me nahi pūrvasammitaḥ purā tvahaṃ ṣaṇṇavatiplavo'smi 
tataḥ kumāro'ṅgada āha cāsmācchataṃ plaveyaṃ na tato'bhijāne   
apūrite taiḥ sakalaiḥ śatasya gamāgame śatrubalaṃ ca vīkṣya 
sudurgamatvaṃ ca niśācareśapuryāḥ sa dhātuḥ suta ābabhāṣe   
ayaṃ hi gṛdhraḥ śatayojanaṃ giriṃ trikūṭamāheta utātra vighnāḥ 
bhaveyuranye'pi tato hanūmānekaḥ samartho na paro'sti kaścit   
uktvā sa itthaṃ punarāha sūnuṃ prāṇasya niḥ sīmabalaṃ praśaṃ sayan 
lvitvameka evātra paraṃ samarthaḥ kuruṣva caitat paripāhi vānarān   
itīrito'sau hanumān nijepsitaṃ teṣāmaśaktiṃ prakaṭāṃ vidhāya 
avardhatā'śu pravicintya rāmaṃ supūrṇaṇsaktiṃ caritostadājñām

atha saptamo'dhyāyaḥ
Oṃ  rāmāya śāṇsvatasuvistṛtaṣaḍguṇāya sarveśvarāya sukhasāramahārṇavāya 
natvā lilaṅghayiṣurarṇavamutpapāta niṣpīḍya taṃ girivaraṃ pavanasya sūnuḥ   
cukṣobha vāridhiranuprayayau ca śīghraṃ yādogaṇaiḥ saha tadīyabalābhikṛṣṭaḥ 
vṛkṣāṇsca parvatagatāḥ pavanena pūrvaṃ kṣipto'rṇave girirudāgamadasya hetoḥ   
syālo harasya giripakṣavināṇsakāle kṣiptvā'rṇave sa marutorvaritātmapakṣaḥ 
haimo giriḥ pavanajasya tu viśramārthamudbhidya vāridhimavarddhadanekasānuḥ   
naivātra viśramaṇamaicchata niḥ śramo'sau niḥ sīmapauruṣaguṇasya kutaḥ śramo'sya 
āṇsliṣya parvatavaraṃ sa dadarśa gacchan devaistu nāgajananīṃ prahitāṃ vareṇa

āsyaṃ praviśya sapadi praviniḥ sṛto'smād devānanandayaduta svṛtameṣu rakṣan   
dṛṣṭvā surapraṇayitāṃ balamasya cograṃ devāḥ pratuṣṭuvuramuṃ sumanobhivṛṣṭyā 
tairādṛtaḥ punarasau viyataiva gacchan chāyāgrahaṃ pratidadarśa ca siṃ hikākhyam

ruddho'nayā'śvatha vijitya ca tāṃ svamuṣṭipiṣṭāṃ tayā'numata eva viveśa laṅkām

dadarśa śiṃ śapāvṛkṣamūlasthitaramākṛtim

lviiit ādṛkceṣṭāsametāyā aṅgulīyamadāt tataḥ   
sīt āyā yāni caivā'sannākṛtestāni sarvaśaḥ 
bhūṣaṇāni dvidhā bhūtvā tānyevā'saṃ stathaiva ca   
atha cūl  āmaṇiṃ divyaṃ dātuṃ rāmāya sā dadau 
yadyapyetanna paśyanti niśācaragaṇāstu te 
dyulokacāriṇaḥ sarvaṃ paśyantyṛṣaya eva ca   
teṣāṃ viḍambanāyaiva daityānāṃ vañcanāya ca 
paśyatāṃ kalimukhyānāṃ viḍambo'yaṃ kṛto bhavet   
kṛtvā kāryamidaṃ sarvaṃ viśaṅkaḥ pavanātmajaḥ 
ātmāviṣkaraṇe cittaṃ cakre matimatāṃ varaḥ   
atha vanamakhilaṃ tad rāvaṇasyāvalupya kṣitiruhamimamekaṃ varjayitvā'śu vīraḥ 
rajanicaravināṇsaṃ kāṅkṣamāṇo'tivelaṃ muhuratiravanādī toraṇaṃ cā'ruroha   
athāṇsṛṇod daśānanaḥ kapīndraceṣṭitaṃ param 
dideśa kiṅkarān bahūn kapirnigṛhyatāmiti   
samastaśo vimṛtyavo varāddharasya kiṅkarāḥ 
samāsadan mahābalam surāntarātmano'ṅgajam   
aṇsītikoṭiyūthapaṃ purassarāṣṭakāyutam 
anekahetisaṅkulaṃ kapīndramāvṛṇod balam   
samāvṛtastathā'yudhaiḥ sa tāḍitaśca tairbhṛśam 
cakāra tān samastaśastal  aprahāracūrṇit ān

kumāramakṣamātmanaḥ samaṃ sutaṃ nyayojayat

śitairvarāstramantritairna cainamabhyacālayat

yadīndrajinmayā hato na cāsya śaktirīkṣyate   
atastayoḥ samo mayā tṛtīya eṣa hanyate 
vicārya caivamāṇsu taṃ padoḥ pragṛhya pupluve

vicūrṇite dharātal  e nije sute sa rāvaṇaḥ

prakopitasya tasya kaḥ purasthitau kṣamo bhavet

Oṃ  śrutvā hanūmaduditaṃ kṛtamasya sarvaṃ prītaḥ prayāṇamabhirocayate sa rāmaḥ

ūcustathaināmudare vayaṃ te jāyemahi kṣipramasmān hana tvam

sa sarvavittvaṃ samavāpya rāmāt samastavidyādhipaterguṇārṇavāt 
pituṃ samīpaṃ samavāpya taṃ ca śuśrūṣamāṇaḥ pramumoda vīraḥ

athā'ha bhīṣmakaṃ prabhuḥ svayaṃ varaḥ kila tvayā 
abhīpsitaḥ sutākṛte śubhāya te bhavenna saḥ   
iyaṃ ramā tavā'tmajā babhūva tāṃ harernaca 
dadāti cet tadā pitā nirindiro vrajedadhaḥ   
hitāya caitadīritaṃ tavānyathā na cintaya 
na yoṣidicchayā tvahaṃ bravīmi paśya yādṛśaḥ   
udīrya caivamīśvaraścakāra hā'virātmanaḥ 
sa viśvarūpamuttamaṃ visaṅkhyaśīrṣabāhukam   
anantateja ātataṃ visaṅkhyarūpasaṃ yutam 
vicitramaulikuṇḍalāṅgadoruhāranūpuram   
jvalatsukaustubhaprabhā'bhibhāsakaṃ śubhāmbaram 
prapaśya yādṛśāḥ striyo mametyadarśayacchriyam   
anantarūpiṇīṃ parāṃ manuṣyadṛṣṭito'dhikām 
svarugmiṇītanorapi vyadarśayacca devatāḥ   
clxxxtadadbhutaṃ samīkṣya tu prabhīta āṇsu bhīṣmakaḥ 
papāta pādayorvibhoḥ karomi tat tatheti ca   
punaśca viśvarūpatāṃ pidhāya padmalocanaḥ 
jagāma pakṣivāhanaḥ purīṃ svabāhupālitām   
apāmpatiśca maithilaḥ svayaṃ varaṅkṛt āvapi 
hariṃ viniścayādiyaṃ vrajediti sma cakratuḥ   
svayaṃ varaḥ kṣiterbhujāṃ svadharma ityato dvayoḥ 
na doṣa āsa bhīṣmako na keśavārthamaicchata   
ato harau prabodhya taṃ gate kṛpālusattame 
vaśīkṛte ca bhīṣmake nṛpāstvamantrayan punaḥ   
yaśaśca dharmamuttamaṃ vidhitsatā vṛkodare 
na keśavena sūdito jarāsuto hi manyate   
varācchivasya māmayaṃ na hantumīṣṭa uttamāt 
ataḥ śivaprasādato jito'pi jeṣya uttaram   
mṛdhemṛdhe jito'pi san dṛḍhāṇsayā punaḥ punaḥ 
samīhate yudhe śivaṃ nacāvamanyate kvacit   
ataḥ punaśca bhūmipānuvāca bārhadrathaḥ 
dhigeva pauruṣaṃ hi no yadeṣa no'jayat sadā   
abhūpaternacā'sanaṃ pradeyamityudāhṛtam 
amuṣya nastadanyathā babhūva cintitaṃ nṛpāḥ   
ayaṃ nṛpottamāṅgaṇe mahendrapīṭhamāruhat 
samastarājarājatāmavāpa no'pyanicchatām   
ataḥ punaḥ kathaṃ hariṃ vayaṃ jayema cintyatām 
yathā cabhīṣmakātmajāmavāpnuyācca cedirāṭ  
clxxxiayaṃ hi dattaputrako ma aurasād viśiṣyate 
ato niveśya eṣa me surūpiṇī ca rugmiṇī   
śivāgameṣu ṇsiṣyakāḥ sarugmisālvapauṇḍrakāḥ 
mamākhilā nṛpāstataḥ kurudhvametadeva me   
itīrite tu saubharāḍjagāda rugmisaṃ vidā 
svayaṃ varo nivartitaḥ svasārameṣa dāsyati   
nacātivartituṃ kṣamaḥ pitā'sya cedipāya tām 
pradātukāmamātmajaṃ vayogatastathā'balaḥ   
svayaṃ tu kṛṣṇa etya no vijitya kanyakāṃ haret 
tato'sya pūrvameva no hyabhāvatā kṛt ā ṇsubhā   
upāya eṣa cintito mayā'tra māgadheśvara 
muniṃ hi garganāmakaṃ hyamuṣya sāla ākṣipat   
yadā'sya ṣaṇḍhatoditā muneḥ puro hi tasya ca 
pareṇa vṛṣṇayo'hasaṃ ścukopa garga eṣu ha  
cakāra hi pratiśravaṃ samārjaye sutaṃ drutam 
akṛṣṇatāṃ ya ānayed bhuvo'pi vṛṣṇināṇsakaḥ   
yato hi kṛṣṇasaṃ śrayād batāpahāsitā vayam 
iti bruvan vanaṃ yayau tapaśca śaivamācarat   
sa cūrṇamāyasaṃ tvadan dadarśa cābdataḥ śivam 
varaṃ tato'bhipedivān sutaṃ harerabhāvadam   
sa viṣṇudaivato'pi san praviṣṭa ulbaṇāsuraiḥ 
vyadhāddhareḥ pratīpakaṃ vrataṃ ca naiṣṭhikaṃ jahau   
tamāra cā'surāpsarā baliṣṭhaputrakāmyayā 
clxxxiipraviśya gopikāṅganāsamūhamadhyamulbaṇā   
sa yāvanena bhūbhṛt ā hi gopikābhirarcitaḥ 
aputrakeṇa jānatā munermano'nucintitam   
sa cāpsarastanau sutaṃ niṣicya yāvanāya ca 
dadau vimohitaḥ krudhā kimetadīśa vairiṇaḥ   
sa āṇsramācca naiṣṭhikād vidūṣitaḥ pratīpakṛt 
hareśca tāpameyivān jagarha cā'tmaśemuṣīm   
jagāma cāraṇaṃ hariṃ prapāhi māṃ supāpinam 
iti sma viṣṇvanujñayā cakāra vaiṣṇavaṃ tapaḥ   
kuto hi bhāgyamāpatenmuneḥ śivārcane sadā 
bhavādṛśā hidānavāḥ sthirāḥ śivārcane sadā   
suto'sya kālanāmako babhūva kṛṣṇamarditum 
sadaiva kālakāṅkṣaṇāt sa yāvanābhiṣecitaḥ   
tavaiva śiṣya eṣa cātibhaktimān hi śaṅkare 
prabhūtasenayā yuto baloddhataśca sarvadā   
tameṣa yāmi śāsanāt tavopanīya satvaram 
vikṛṣṇakaṃ kṣitestal  aṃ vidhāya saṃ ramāma hā   
tataśca rugmiṇīṃ vayaṃ pradāpayāma cedipe 
vināṇsya devapakṣiṇo yatheṣṭamāsma sarvadā   
itīrito jarāsuto babhūva durmanā bhṛśam 
kirīṭamaṇḍitaṃ śiraścakāra cā'śvavāg bhṛśam   
karaṃ kareṇa pīḍayan niśāmya cā'tmano bhujau 
jagāda kāryasiddhaye kathaṃ prayācaye param   
clxxxiiisudurgakāryasantatiṃ hyaguḥ sma madbhujāṇsrayāḥ 
samastabhūtal  e nṛpāḥ sa cāhameṣa māgadhaḥ   
kadā'pyacīrṇamadya tat kathaṃ karomi kevalam 
girīśapādasaṃ śrayaḥ prabhuḥ samastabhūbhṛt ām   
itīritaḥ sa saubharāḍjagāda vākyamuttaram 
bhavānapi sma muhyate kimasmadādayaḥ prabho   
svaśiṣyakaiḥ kṛtaṃ tu yat kimanyasādhitaṃ bhavet 
svaśiṣyadāsavargakaiḥ samarthayanti bhūbhujaḥ   
api sma te balāṇsrayapravṛttayo'smadādayaḥ 
pumān kuṭhārasaṅgrahādaśakta īryate hi kim   
kuṭhārasammito hyasau tavaiva yāvaneśvaraḥ 
vinā bhavadbalaṃ kvacit pravartituṃ nahi kṣamaḥ   
varo hi kṛṣṇamardane vṛto'sya kevalaḥ śivāt 
tadanyaśatrupīḍanāt tvameva tasya rakṣakaḥ   
tavākhilairajeyatā ṇsivaprasādato'sti hi 
viśeṣato harerjaye varādayaṃ vimārgyate   
itīrite'pyatṛptavat sthite tu bārhadrathe 
jagāma saubhamāsthitaḥ sa saubharāṭca yāvanam   
sa kālayāvano'tha taṃ jarāsutāntikāgatam 
niśamya bhaktipūrvakaṃ praṇamya cā'rcayad drutam   
jarāsuto hi daivataṃ samastakeśavadviṣām 
iti praṇamya tāṃ diśaṃ tadīyamāṇsvapūjayat   
tadīritaṃ niśamya ca drutaṃ trikoṭisaṅkhyayā 
akṣohiṇīkayā yutaḥ svasenayā nirākramat   
clxxxivtadaśvamūtraviṣṭhayā babhūva nāmata śakṛt 
nadī suvegagāminī kalau ca yā vahed drutam   
punaḥ punarnadībhavaṃ niśāmya deśasaṅkṣayam 
tadanyadeśamūtritaṃ vyaśoṣayaddhi mārutaḥ   
hariśca vainateyayug vicārya rāmasaṃ yutaḥ 
sadā'tipūrṇasaṃ vidapyajo'tha līlayā'smarat   
yuyutsureṣa yāvanaḥ samīpamāgato'dya naḥ 
yuyutsatāmanena no jarāsuto'bhiyāsyati   
sa yādavān haniṣyati prabhaṅgatastu kopitaḥ 
purā jayāṇsayā hi nau yadūn na jaghnivānasau   
nirāṇsako'dya yādavānapi sma pīḍayiṣyati 
ataḥ samudramadhyagāpurīvidhānamadya me 
prarocate nidhānamapyamutra sarvasāttvatām   
udīrya caivamīśvaro'smarat sureśavardhakim 
sa bhauvanaḥ samāgataḥ kuśasthalīṃ vinirmame   
nirambuke tu sāgare janārdanājñayā kṛte 
mahodakasya madhyataścakāra tāṃ purīṃ śubhām 
dviṣaṭkayojanāyatāṃ payobdhimadhyagopamām   
cakāra lāvaṇodakaṃ janārdano'mṛtopamam 
sabhāṃ sudharmanāmakāṃ dadau samīraṇo'sya ca   
śatakratoḥ sabhāṃ tu tāṃ pradāya keśavāya saḥ 
nidhīn samarpya sarvaśo yayau praṇamya taṃ prabhum   
samastadevatāgaṇāḥ svakīyamarpayan harau 
vimucya pakṣipuṅgavaṃ sa yoddhumaicchadacyutaḥ   
clxxxvsamastamādhurān prabhuḥ kuśasthalīsthitān kṣaṇāt 
vidhāya bāhuyodhakaḥ sa yāvanaṃ samabhyayāt   
anantaśaktirapyajaḥ sunītidṛṣṭaye nṛṇām 
vyavāsayannijān janān sa līlayaiva kevalam   
anādyanantakālakaṃ samastalokamaṇḍalam 
yadīkṣayaiva rakṣyate kimasya vṛṣṇirakṣaṇam   
nirāyudhaṃ ca māmayaṃ varācchivasya na kṣamaḥ 
samastasenayā yuto'pi yoddhumityadarśayat   
sa kṛṣṇapannagaṃ ghaṭe nidhāya keśavo'rpayat

bahutvato vijeṣya ityahiṃ mṛtaṃ vyadarśayat   
kimatra satyamityahaṃ pradarśayiṣya ityajaḥ 
udīrya dūtamabhyayāt sa yāvanaṃ prabādhitum   
sa bāhunaiva keśavo vijitya yāvanaṃ prabhuḥ 
nihatya sarvasainikān svamasya yāpayat purīm   
sahāstraśastrasañcayān sṛjantamāṇsu yāvanam

vivāhanaṃ nirāyudhaṃ vidhāya bāhunā kṣaṇāt

clxxxviariṃ bhaviṣyayāvanaṃ dahatvayaṃ taveśvara

sa yāvanaḥ padā'hanannṛpaṃ sa taṃ dadarśa ha

clxxxviisasañjñakāḥ samutthitāstato nṛpāḥ punaryayuḥ

Oṃ  evaṃ śubhoccaguṇavatsu janārdanena yukteṣu pāṇḍuṣu caratsvadhikaṃ śubhāni 
nāstikyanītimakhilāṃ gurudevatādisatsvañjasaiva jagṛhurdhṛtarāṣṭraputrāḥ

nītiṃ sa kutsitatamāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraputreṣvādhād raho vacanataḥ śakuneḥ samastām   
chadmaiva yatra paramaṃ na surāṇsca pūjyāḥ svārthena vañcanakṛte jagato'khilaṃ ca 
dharmādi kāryamapi yasya mahopādhiḥ syācchreṣṭhaḥ sa eva nikhilāsuradaityasaṅghāt   
ityādi kutsitatamāṃ jagṛhuḥ sma vidyāmajñāta eva dhṛtarāṣṭramukhaiḥ samastaiḥ 
teṣāṃ svabhāvabalato rucitā ca saiva vistāritā ca nijabuddhibalādato'pi

dṛṣṭvā ṇsriyaṃ paramikāṃ vijayaṃ ca pārtheṣvāhedametya pitaraṃ saha saubalena   
jyeṣṭhasya te'pi hi vayaṃ hṛdayaprajātā nārhatvameva gamitā bhavataiva rājye 
bhrātuḥ kanīyasa utāpi hi dārajātā anyaiśca rājyapadavīṃ bhavataiva nīt āḥ   
rājyaṃ mahacca samavāpsyati dharmasūnustvatto'thavā'nujabalāt prasabhaṃ vayaṃ tu 
dāsā bhavema nijatantubhireva sākaṃ kuntīsutasya parato'pi tadanvayasya   
nā'tmārthamasti mama duḥkhamathātiśuddhalokaprasiddhayaśasastava kīrtināṇsaḥ 
asmannimitta iti duḥkhamato hi sarve'pīcchāma martumatha naḥ kuru cāpyanujñām   
evaṃ svaputravacanaṃ sa niśamya rājā provāca nānuguṇametadaho manaste 
ko nāma pāṇḍutanayeṣu guṇottameṣu prītiṃ na yāti nijavīryabhavoccayeṣu

saṃ yodhayāmāsurathābhyavarṣaccharairniṣādādhipa ekalavyaḥ   
tadastraśastraiḥ sahasā viṣaṇṇā yadupravīrā vihatapradīpāḥ 
sahaiva rāmeṇa ṇsineśca naptrā samāviśan svāṃ purameva sarve   
punaḥ samādāya tathorudīpikā agre samādhāya ca rauhiṇeyam 
vinissṛt ā āttaśastrāḥ svapuryāḥ siṃ hā yathā dharṣit āḥ sadguhāyāḥ   
athā'sasādaikalavyaṃ rathena rāmaḥ śaineyaḥ pauṇḍrakaṃ vāsudevam 
ayuddhyatāṃ tau sātyakiḥ pauṇḍrakaśca tathā'nyonyaṃ virathaṃ cakratuśca    
tato gadāyuddhamabhūt tayordvayostathā rāmaścaikalavyaśca vīrau 
kṛtvā'nyonyaṃ virathaṃ gadābhyāmayuddhyatāṃ j ātadarpau balāgryau   
tasmin kāle keśavo vainateyamāruṃ hyā'yād yatra te yuddasaṃ sthāḥ 
dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ harṣasampūritātmā rāmo hantuṃ caikalavyaṃ samaicchat   
udyamya dorbhyāṃ sa gadāṃ javenaivābhyāpatad rauhiṇeyo niṣādam 
balaṃ kopaṃ cāsya dṛṣṭvaikalavyaḥ parādravajjīvitecchuḥ sudūram   
vidrāvayan rauhiṇeyo'nvayāt taṃ bhīto'pataccaikalavyo'mbudhau saḥ 
velāntaṃ taṃ drāvayitvā'tra tasthau rāmo gadāpāṇiradīnasattvaḥ

cccxiisupāpo'sāvekalavyaḥ subhīto rāmaṃ matvaivānuyātaṃ punaśca

prasthāpayāmāsa punaśca dūtaṃ kṛṣṇāyaiko vāsudevo'hamasmi

anye ca daityā apataṃ stamo'ndhe tathaiva so'pyapatat pāpabuddhiḥ   
nihatya tau keśavo raugmiṇeyaṃ punarvaidarbhyāṃ janayāmāsa sadyaḥ

cccxiiievaṃ yadūnāmṛṣabheṇa sūdite pauṇḍre tathā kāṇsinṛpe ca pāpe

j ājvalyamānaṃ tadamoghavīryaṃ vyadrāvayad vahnimimaṃ sudūram

striyā bhetavyaṃ bharturityeva dharmaṃ vijñāpayantī duḥkhitevā'sa devī 
t āṃ sāntvayāmāsa gṛhasthadharmaṃ vijñāpayan devadevo'pyaduḥkhām

cccxivtadaiva maindo vividaśca bhaume hate sakhāyau dānavāveśayuktau 
ānartarāṣṭraṃ vāsudevapratīpau vyanāṇsayetāṃ vāsudevo'tha coce

kṛcchreṇa taṃ virathīkṛtya caikaṃ sarve sametā jagṛhurdhārtarāṣṭrāḥ 
karṇena bhūriśravasā casārddhaṃ bāhvorbalādeva duryodhanasya

purasya bāhyopavane sthitaḥ sa prāsthāpayaccoddhavaṃ kauravārthe 
āgatya sarve kuravo'sya pūjāṃ cakruḥ sa cā'hograsenasya cā'jñām   
ājñāpayad vo nṛpatiḥ sma yannaḥ kumārakaḥ pragṛhīto bhavadbhiḥ 
ekaḥ sametairbahubhirbāndhavārthaṃ kṣāntaṃ tanno muñcatā'śveva sāmbam   
ājñāpayāmāsa va ugrasena ityuktameva tu niśamya kurupravīrāḥ 
saṃ śrāvya duṣṭavacanāni balaṃ puraṃ svaṃ krodhāt samāviviśuratra cukopa rāmaḥ   
sa lāṅgalena tat puraṃ vikṛṣya jāhnavījale 
nipātayan nivāritaḥ praṇamya sarvakauravaiḥ

cccxvityādikarmāṇi mahānti rāmasyā'sañcheṣasyācyutāveśino'lam

tadā bhīmo vijayī syāt sadaiva viṣṇoḥ keśāveśavān yat sa rāmaḥ   
etādṛśenaiva rāmeṇa yukte kṛṣṇe dvārvatyāṃ nivasatyabjanābhe

gūḍhaṃ kanyāgṛhe taṃ tu jñātvā kanyābhirakṣiṇaḥ

yuddhvaivāṅgirasā caiva kṣaṇād vidrāpya tān hariḥ

tena bhasmaprahāreṇa jvaritaṃ rohiṇīsutam 
āṇsliṣya vijvaraṃ cakre vāsudevo jagatprabhuḥ   
cccxvisvayaṃ vikrīḍya tenātha kañcit kālaṃ janārdanaḥ 
niṣpiṣya muṣṭibhiścānyaṃ sasarja jvaramacyutaḥ

svabhṛtyenaiva jetavya ityanyaṃ sasṛje tadā

tena stutaḥ sa bhagavān mocayāmāsa taṃ vibhuḥ

tayorabhūd yuddhamathainamacyuto vijṛmbhayāmāsa ha jṛmbhaṇāstrataḥ

cccxviiīdṛśānantasaṅkhyānāṃ śivānāṃ brahmaṇāmapi

naca jñānādayo bhāvā nacāstitvamapi kvacit

citralekhāsametoṣānvitapautrasamanvitaḥ

reme tatra ciraṃ kṛṣṇo nityānando nijecchayā   
evaṃ vidhānyagaṇit āni yadūttamasya karmāṇyagaṇyamahimasya mahotsavasya 
nityaṃ ramākamalajanmagirīśaśakrasūryādibhiḥ parinutāni vimuktidāni   
evaṃ vasatyamitapauruṣavīryasāre nārāyaṇe svapuri śakradhanañjayoktaḥ 
samprāpya lomaśamuniḥ sakalāni tīrthānyāptuṃ sa pāṇḍutanayeṣu sahāya āsīt   
pṛthvīṃ pradakṣiṇata etya samastatīrthasnānaṃ yathākramata eva vidhāya pārthāḥ 
sampūjya teṣu nikhileṣu hariṃ subhaktyā kṛṣṇe samarpayitumāpuratha prabhāsam 
sambhāvanāya sakalairyadubhiḥ sametasteṣāṃ ca rāmasahito harirājagāma

pārthān sampūjayāmāsurvṛṣṇayaścā'jñayā hareḥ   
tatra bhīmaṃ tapoveṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā'tisnehakāraṇāt 
duryodhanaṃ nindayati rāme sātyakirabravīt   
sarve vayaṃ nihatyādya sakarṇān dhṛtarāṣṭraj ān 
abhimanyuṃ sthāpayāmo rājye yāvat trayodaśam   
saṃ vatsaraṃ samāpyaiva puraṃ yāsyanti pāṇḍavāḥ 
tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā rājyaṃ śāsatu pūrvavat   
evaṃ vadatyeva śinipravīre janārdanaḥ pārthamukhānyudīkṣya 
uvāca śaineya na pāṇḍuputrāḥ pareṇa saṃ sādhitarājyakāmāḥ   
cccxviiisvabāhuvīryeṇa nihatya śatrūnāpsyanti rājyaṃ ta itīrite'munā

tatpakṣavātena vicālite tu tasmin girau kamalaṃ haimamagryam

tayā'rthitaḥ sagadastuṅgamenaṃ giriṃ vegādāruhad vāyusūnuḥ 
praśasyamānaḥ surasiddhasaṅghaiḥ mṛtnan daityān siṃ haśārdūlarūpān   
āsedivāṃ statra hanūmadākhyaṃ nijaṃ rūpaṃ prodyadādityabhāsam 
j ānannapyenaṃ svīyarūpaṃ sa bhīmaścikrīḍa etena yathā pareṇa   
dharmo devānāṃ paramo mānuṣatve svīye rūpe'pyanyavadeva vṛttiḥ 
anādānaṃ divyaśakterviśeṣānnarasvabhāve sarvadā caiva vṛttiḥ

cccxixsarve guṇā āvṛt ā mānuṣatve yugānusārānmūlarūpānusārāt 
kramāt surāṇāṃ bhāgato'vyaktarūpā ādānato vyaktimāyāntyurūṇām   
naivāvyaktiḥ kācidastīha viṣṇoḥ prādurbhāve'pyatisuvyaktaśakteḥ 
icchāvyaktiḥ prāyaśo mārutasya tadanyeṣāṃ vyaktatā kāraṇena

tadrūpavṛddhiṃ bhīmaseno'tha dṛṣṭvā ṇsrutvā hanūmanmukhataḥ kathāṇsca

dhvajād bībhatsorgarjanenaiva śatruparābhave tena datte'rjunasya

te bhīmamāttāyudhamugrarūpaṃ mahābalaṃ rūpanavāvatāram

bhīme'khilajñe tapasāṃ nidhāne balodadhau śaivaśāstraṃ vadantaḥ   
t ān vaiṣṇavaireva śāstraiḥ sa bhīmo vijitya pūrvaṃ vāṅmaye saṅgare tu 
śāstrāstravarṣasya kurvan pratīpaṃ jaghne'khilān gadayā teṣu vīrān

satye ca dharme ca rataḥ sadaiva parākrame śatrubhirapradhṛṣyaḥ   
tatrāparāṃ ścaiva bahūnasatyaṃ nirīśvaraṃ cāpratiṣṭhaṃ ca lokam 
siddho'hamīśo'hamiti bruvāṇān guṇān viṣṇoḥ khyāpayan vādato'jait   
bhinnaṃ viṣṇumadhikaṃ sarvataśca bruvan pravīrān lakṣameṣāṃ nijaghne 
te tasya vīryaṃ ca balaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā vidyābalaṃ bāhubalaṃ tathaiva 
cccxxaṇsaknuvantaḥ sahitāḥ samastā hatapravīrāḥ sahasā nivṛtt āḥ
